## PAGE 01733: Producing and Consuming Functions dialog

- page_id: `249575948`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575948/Producing+and+Consuming+Functions+dialog
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-08-26T15:17:06.388+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > Dialogs
- labels: ['producing-and-consuming-functions-dialog']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

The**Producing and Consuming Functions** dialog allows you to specify or modify producing and consuming Functions for a selected Resource Interaction.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

To open the **Producing and Consuming Functions** dialog

- In the Specification window of the Resource Interaction, click the Edit (...) button in the selected Producing Function or Consuming Function cell.
- In the SV-6 Systems Data Exchange Matrix, click the Edit (...) button in the selected Producing Function or Consuming Function cell.
- In the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Resource Interaction Manager dialog' space='UPDM2P']**Resource Interaction Manager dialog** : - Click the **Edit** (...) button in the selected **Producing Function or Consuming Function** cell. - Click the **Functions** button.

The **Producing and Consuming Functions** dialog is embedded in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Realized Resource Interaction wizard' space='UPDM2P']**Realized Resource Interaction** wizardas a step #2.

Elements of the dialog are described in the following tables.

| Box | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Update Diagrams | Select to update all related diagrams. Existing diagrams will be updated by displaying a particular resource interaction as a triangle on every Function Edge connecting producing and consuming function actions. If the specified Producing and Consuming Functions does not exist in any diagram, you will be suggested to create a new SV-4 System Functionality Description Flow (DoDAF), SV-4 Functionality Description Flow (MODAF), or NSV-4 System Functionality Description Flow (NAF) diagram. Producing and Consuming Function actions and the Resource Interaction will be represented in this new diagram. |

| Button | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Add | Click to add a new row for assigning a pair of Producing and Consuming Functions. |
| Remove From Table | Click to delete a selected Producing and Consuming Functions pair. |
| Show Full Paths | Click to show views containing specified functions (see the following figure).Click once again to hide this information. |

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

To specify a pair of producing and consuming functions

1. In the**Producing Function** column of a selected row, create a new value:
  - Click the drop-down arrow to open a list of available functions and select one. If you do not see the list of available functions, click [IMAGE alt='' src=''] and select the **Performed Functions** button.
  - Click the “ ... ” button to create a new or select a function existing in the model. The Select Function dialog opens, wherein you are able to select or create functions.
2. Perform the same action described above for the **Consuming Function** column of the same row.

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Filtering Operational Activities and Functions' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Realized Resource Interaction wizard' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Resource Interaction Manager dialog' space='UPDM2P']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

1338991974

1338991976

1338991975

##### Description

MODAF/NAF: A Project (MODAF::ProjectType, NAF::ProjectType) is used to define a category of project: For example, “Program”, “Acquisition Project” or “Training Program”.

DoDAF: NA (only Individual Project in DoDAF).

##### Architecture Framework

MODAF, DoDAF, NAF

##### Extensions

UML Class

1339329081

1339329084

1339329083

##### Description

UPDM: An element representing a collection of themes (e.g., DLOD or DOTMLPF) which is connected to a Project as part of a Project’s definition. This is used as a template for ActualProjectMilestones.

MODAF/NAF: An event in a Project by which progress is measured.

##### Architecture Framework

MODAF, DoDAF, NAF

##### Extensions

UML Class

1343230442

##### Description

MODAF/NAF: A ProjectStatus (MODAF::StatusAtMilestone, NAF::StatusAtMilestone) is a relationship between a Status and a milestone that asserts the status (i.e., level of progress) of a ProjectTheme for the project at the time of the ActualProjectMilestone (MODAF::Milestone, NAF::Milestone).

DoDAF: NA

##### Architecture Framework

MODAF, DoDAF, NAF

##### Extensions

UML Slot

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575951 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01741: Project Status Application Wizard

- page_id: `249575951`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575951/Project+Status+Application+Wizard
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-08-10T10:55:34.121+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > Dialogs
- labels: ['project-status-application-wizard']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

The **Project Status Application Wizard** is used to apply the DLOD Milestone, DOTMLPF Milestone, or custom Milestone type to the selected element, which can be one of the following:

- Out Of Service Milestone
- Increment Milestone
- Deployed Milestone
- No Longer Used Milestone
- Actual Project Milestone

To open the **Project Status Application Wizard**

1. Right-click the Milestone and select Edit Status . The Project Status Application Wizard opens.

The wizard consists of two steps:

1. Select an Actual Project Milestone Type. How to select an Actual Project Milestone Type?In this step, select DLOD Milestone, DOTMLPF Milestone, or create your own Milestone type.[IMAGE alt='' src='']
2. Specify Project Status at a particular Milestone. How to specify Project Status at a particular Milestone?In this step, specify project threads and status indicators of the selected Actual Project Milestone Type.[IMAGE alt='' src='']Project threadsStatus indicators**DLOD Milestone type**EquipmentLogisticsInfrastructureOrganizationDoctrine/ConceptsInformationPersonnelTrainingDLOD AbsentNot RequiredNo Outstanding IssuesManageable IssuesCritical Issues[IMAGE alt='' src='']Project threadsStatus indicators**DOTMLPF Milestone type**DoctrineOrganizationTrainingMaterielLeadershipPersonnelFacilitiesMateriel Solution AnalysisTechnology DevelopmentEngineering and Manufacturing DevelopmentProduction & DeploymentOperations & SupportIf you selected your own milestone type, you can create your own projects threads and status indicators.To create project threads and status indicators1. In the Project Thread area, click the **Add** button.2. Specify the thread name.3. In the Status Indicator area, click the **Add** button.4. Specify the indicator name.5. Click the **Fill Color** button.6. In the **Color dialog** choose the color and click **OK**.To create a second thread with the same status indicators, select a previously created thread and click the **Clone**button. A new thread with previously defined status indicators is created.To remove the applied Project Status1. Click [IMAGE alt='' src=''] in the right bottom corner.

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

## PAGE 01744: Project viewpoint

- page_id: `249575135`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575135/Project+viewpoint
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:40:44.983+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views
- labels: ['project-viewpoint']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

1416628093

1416628095

1416628094

“The DoDAF-described Models within the Project Viewpoint describe how programs, projects, portfolios, or initiatives deliver capabilities, the organizations contributing to them, and dependencies between them. Previous versions of DoDAF took a traditional model of architecture in which descriptions of programs and projects were considered outside scope. To compensate for this, various DoDAF models represented the evolution of systems, technologies and standards (e.g., Systems and Services Evolution Description, Systems Technology Forecast, and Technical Standards Forecast).” [DoDAF V2.0 Volume II]

1416628092

**Related Pages:**

##### Description

UPDM: Asserts that a Resource type provides a competence.

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249576032 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01749: Publishing project as web portal

- page_id: `249576032`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249576032/Publishing+project+as+web+portal
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2022-06-27T11:39:39.278+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > Procedures > Managing Reports
- labels: ['interactive-web-portal', 'publish-project-as-web-portal']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

Publish your project as interactive web portal and share it with stakeholders, including even those incapable of reading models in MagicDraw! The published web portal eliminates less needed elements from the model tree and proposes the most relevant views of enterprise architecture project, such as capability/strategic, operational, systems, services, standards, projects. This allows you to discover your project in a user-friendly and easily browsable environment.

If you want to publish a project as a web portal, you must install the Document Modeling Plugin. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Installing plugins' space='NMDOC']>]]>

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

You can also provide feedback on any element or diagram while reviewing an Enterprise Architecture Portal report of the project.

Use quick search to find elements and diagrams for viewing their custom contents and share this information with colleagues.

Publishing the project as a web portal is as easy as generating any report.

To publish a project

1. On the main menu, click Tools > Report Wizard .
2. Select one of the following templates:
  - DoDAF > DoDAF Web Report
  - MODAF > MODAF Web Report
  - NAF > NAF Web Report
  - NAF 4 > NAF 4.0 Web Report
3. Follow the steps of the Report Wizard .
4. Place the output in a shared directory or on web server to make it available for co-workers.

The following table introduces what you can expect in your web report. In every view of the report, you may find the following information:

- What elements are collected
- Collected element properties
- Related elements
- Related diagram types

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575136 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01750: PV-1 Project Portfolio Relationships

- page_id: `249575136`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575136/PV-1+Project+Portfolio+Relationships
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:19:33.301+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Project viewpoint
- labels: ['pv-1', 'pv-1-project-portfolio-relationships', 'pv-1-responsibility-matrix']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

29186712

29186714

29186713

**Description**

The PV-1 represents an organizational perspective on programs, projects, portfolios, or initiatives.

The PV-1 enables the user to model the organizational structures needed to manage programs, projects, portfolios, or initiatives. It shows dependency relationships between the actual organizations that own the programs, projects, portfolios, or initiatives. This model could be used to represent organizational relationships associated with transformation initiatives along with those who are responsible for managing programs, projects, and portfolios. The PV-1 provides a means of analyzing the main dependencies between acquisition elements or transformation elements.

The intended usage of the PV-1 includes, but is not limited to:

- Program management (specified acquisition program structure).
- Project organization.
- Cross-cutting initiatives to be tracked across portfolios.

**Implementation**

PV-1 can be represented using:

- A PV-1 Project Portfolio Relationships diagram which is based on the UML Class diagram. [ATTACHMENT filename='PV-1_diagram.png']
- A PV-1 Responsibility Matrix which is an editable Dependency Matrix. [ATTACHMENT filename='AcV-1_PV-1_matrix.PNG']

The model is strongly linked with the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='CV-4 Capability Dependencies' space='UPDM2P'] model which shows capability groupings and dependencies.

29186711

**Related Pages:**

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Actual Organization' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Individual Person Role' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Organizational Project Relationship' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Project' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Project Type' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Project Milestone' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Project Milestone Role' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Actual Project Milestone Role' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Status Indicators' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Project Activity' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Activity Part of Project' space='UPDM2P']

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<ac:structured-macro ac:name="content-layer" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="537e56c3-4745-4dcf-b7bb-13d01fa3fce3"><ac:parameter ac:name="id">29186712</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><ac:structured-macro ac:name="content-column" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="513d6c28-a580-4742-9fc4-0e79320f3cda"><ac:parameter ac:name="id">29186714</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><ac:structured-macro ac:name="content-block" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="6531cc8a-8c5e-4424-86ba-5fa5c69aee15"><ac:parameter ac:name="id">29186713</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p><strong>Description</strong></p><p>The PV-1 represents an organizational perspective on programs, projects, portfolios, or initiatives.</p><p>The PV-1 enables the user to model the organizational structures needed to manage programs, projects, portfolios, or initiatives. It shows dependency relationships between the actual organizations that own the programs, projects, portfolios, or initiatives. This model could be used to represent organizational relationships associated with transformation initiatives along with those who are responsible for managing programs, projects, and portfolios. The PV-1 provides a means of analyzing the main dependencies between acquisition elements or transformation elements.</p><p>The intended usage of the PV-1 includes, but is not limited Relationships" /></ri:attachment></ac:image><br /><br /></li></ul><p>The model is strongly linked with the <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="CV-4 Capability Dependencies" /></ac:link> model which shows capability groupings and dependencies.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ac:structured-macro ac:name="content-block" ac:schema-version="1" <!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575141 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01751: PV-2 Project Timelines

- page_id: `249575141`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575141/PV-2+Project+Timelines
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:07:27.631+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Project viewpoint
- labels: ['pv-2', 'pv-2-project-timelines', 'pv-2-gantt-chart']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

29712997

29712999

29712998

**Description**

The PV-2 provides a timeline perspective on programs. The PV-2 is intended primarily to support the acquisition and fielding processes including the management of dependencies between projects and the integration of DoDD 5000.1 Defense Acquisition System policies to achieve a successfully integrated capability. The PV-2 is not limited to the acquisition and fielding processes.

The intended usage of the PV-2 includes:

- Project management and control (including delivery timescales).
- Project dependency risk identification.
- Management of dependencies.
- Portfolio management.

**Implementation**

PV-2 can be represented using a PV-2 diagram which is realized as a Gantt Chart.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

Use of PV-2 should support the management of capability delivery and be aligned with the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='CV-3 Capability Phasing' space='UPDM2P'] model, if one exists.

29712996

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575152 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01752: PV-3 Project to Capability Mapping

- page_id: `249575152`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575152/PV-3+Project+to+Capability+Mapping
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:09:01.998+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Project viewpoint
- labels: ['pv-3', 'pv-3-project-to-capability-mapping', 'pv-3-matrix']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

35598491

35598493

35598492

**Description**

The PV-3 supports the acquisition and deployment processes, including the management of dependencies between projects and the integration of all relevant project and program elements to achieve a capability.

The PV-3 maps programs, projects, portfolios, or initiatives to capabilities to show how the specific elements help to achieve a capability. Programs, projects, portfolios, or initiatives are mapped to the capability for a particular timeframe. Programs, projects, portfolios, or initiatives may contribute to multiple capabilities and may mature across time. The analysis can be used to identify capability redundancies and shortfalls, highlight phasing issues, expose organizational or system interoperability problems, and support program decisions, such as when to phase out a legacy system.

The intended usage of the PV-3 includes:

- Tracing capability requirements to projects.
- Capability audit.

**Implementation**

PV-3 can be represented using a PV-3 diagram which is a non-editable Dependency Matrix. Capabilities are used as row elements and Actual Projects are used as column elements.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

This model is analogous to the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-5a Operational Activity to Systems Function Traceability Matrix' space='UPDM2P'], but provides the interface between Capability and Project Models rather than Operational to System Models.

35598490

**Related Pages:**

****

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Capability' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Project' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Activity Part of Capability' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Activity Part of Project' space='UPDM2P']

## PAGE 01753: Question dialog

- page_id: `249576012`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249576012/Question+dialog
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-05-21T08:59:45.881+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > Procedures > Converting Model between Enterprise Architecture Frameworks
- labels: ['question-dialog', 'convert-diagram-types', 'convert-element-types', 'convert-template-structure', 'display-project-conversion-confirmation-question']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

The **Question** dialog opens when [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Converting Model between Enterprise Architecture Frameworks' space='UPDM2P'].

The dialog asks whether user wants to convert the model according to specified options or not.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

| Check box | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Convert diagram types | Select to convert all diagram types to corresponding diagram types in the selected framework. |
| Convert element types | Select to convert all element types to their aliases in the selected framework. |
| Convert template structure | Select to convert the template structure to the template structure in the selected framework. |
| Do not show this message again | Select to hide the dialog the next time when performing the model conversion.To restore the usage of the Question dialogClick Options > Environment.In the Environment Options dialog select the UPDM options group.In the General properties, set the Display project conversion confirmation question property value to true. |

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575956 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01754: Realized Operational Exchange wizard

- page_id: `249575956`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575956/Realized+Operational+Exchange+wizard
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-08-10T11:32:21.063+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > Dialogs
- labels: ['realized-operational-exchange-wizard']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

The **Realized Operational Exchange** wizard gives the instructions to follow, when adding a new Operational Exchange or selecting one of the existing Operational Exchanges to:

- A Needline between a pair of Performer usages in OV-2 (NOV-2 in NAF) diagrams.
- An Operational Activity Edge between a pair of Operational Activities in OV-5 (NOV-5 in NAF) behavioral diagram.
- An Operational Message between a pair of two lifelines of Performers in OV-6c (NOV-6c in NAF) diagram.

The **Realized Operational Exchange** wizard includes of two steps:

1. Operational Exchange creation (mandatory). How to create a new or select an existing Operational Exchange?This step is designed to create a new Operational Exchange by specifying a Conveyed Item, both sending and receiving Performers, and a direction of a Operational Exchange. Depending on a fact, if selected Performers are known or not, requested information differs: 
- If sending and receiving Performers are unknown form the wizard invocation context, you need to specify both. 
[IMAGE alt='' src='']- If sending and receiving Performers are known, they are added to a **Realized Operational Exchange** wizard automatically. 
[IMAGE alt='' src='']BoxDescriptionConveyed ItemOne or more Operational Exchange Items that are conveyed by the information flow from the sending Performers to receiving Performers.Operational ExchangeOperational Exchange that specifies an information flow for specified conveyed items.If you select an existing Operational Exchange from the drop-down list, Conveyed Item and Direction boxes will be filled with corresponding information automatically. You will be able to edit values of conveyed items.The direction of the information flow won’t be editable.Available if sending and receiving Performers are known from the wizard invocation context.Sending PerformerPerformer that sends the specified conveyed information.Available if a Performer is unknown from the wizard invocation context.Receiving PerformerPerformer that receives the specified conveyed information.Available if a Performer is unknown from the wizard invocation context.DirectionDirection of the information flow. 
[IMAGE alt='' src='']After changing the direction from the default one, the sending Performance is switched with the receiving Performance. The direction of the Operational Exchange is changed accordingly.Add Operational Exchange to corresponding relationshipsSelect the check box, if you want to add the Operational Exchange to corresponding relationships existing in other related diagrams.ButtonDescription[IMAGE alt='' src=''](by the **Conveyed Item** box)Click to open the **Select Conveyed Information** dialog to select or create a conveyed item. You can specify more than one conveyed item.[IMAGE alt='' src=''](by the **Sending Performer**box)Click to open the element Selection dialog.[IMAGE alt='' src=''](by the **Receiving****Performer**box)Click to open the element Selection dialog.
2. Producing and Consuming Activities specification (optional). How to specify Producing and Consuming Activities?This step is designed to specify Producing and Consuming Activities for the created or selected Operational Exchange. Operational Exchanges are produced and consumed by Activities acting under the Performers.[IMAGE alt='' src='']

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating Operational Exchanges in L1 Node Types diagram' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating Operational Exchanges in L2 Logical Scenario diagram' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating Operational Exchanges in L4 Logical Activities diagram' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating Operational Exchanges in L6 Logical Sequence diagram' space='UPDM2P']
- Creating Operational Exchanges in OV-2 diagram
- Creating Operational Exchanges in OV-2 Internal diagram
- Creating Operational Exchanges in OV-5b diagram
- Creating Operational Exchanges in OV-6c diagram
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Operational Exchange Manager dialog' space='UPDM2P']

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<ac:layout><ac:layout-section ac:type="two_right_sidebar"><ac:layout-cell><p>The <strong>Realized Operational Exchange</strong> wizard gives the instructions to follow, when adding a new Operational Exchange or selecting one of the existing Operational Exchanges to:</p><ul><li>A Needline between a pair of Performer usages in OV-2 (NOV-2 in NAF) diagrams.</li><li>An Operational Activity Edge between a pair of Operational Activities in OV-5 (NOV-5 in NAF) behavioral diagram.</li><li>An Operational Message between a pair of two lifelines of Performers in OV-6c (NOV-6c in NAF) diagram.</li></ul><p>The <strong>Realized Operational Exchange</strong> wizard includes of two steps:</p><ol><li><p>Operational Exchange creation (mandatory).</p><ac:structured-macro ac:macro-id="651cd12a-77f7-4e5d-82b6-54f2c5bdfeb9" ac:name="expand" ac:schema-version="1"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">How to create a new or select an existing Operational Exchange?</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p>This step is designed to create a new Operational Exchange by specifying a Conveyed Item, both sending and receiving Performers, and a direction of a Operational Exchange. Depending on a fact, if selected Performers are known or not, requested information differs:<br />- If sending and receiving Performers are unknown form the wizard invocation context, you need to specify both.<br /><ac:image ac:alt="Creating new or selecting Operational Exchange in Realized Operational Exchange wizard" ac:title="Creating new or selecting Operational Exchange in Realized Operational Exchange wizard"><ri:attachment ri:filename="realized_operational_exchange_wizard_step1_1.png"><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Realized Operational Exchange wizard" /></ri:attachment></ac:image></p><p>- If sending and receiving Performers are known, they are added to a <strong>Realized Operational Exchange</strong> wizard automatically.<br /><ac:image ac:alt="Creating new or selecting Operational Exchange in Realized Operational Exchange wizard" ac:title="Creating new or selecting Operational Exchange in Realized Operational Exchange wizard"><ri:attachment ri:filename="realized_operational_exchange_wizard_step1.png"><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Realized Operational Exchange wizard" /></ri:attachment></ac:image></p><p> </p><table><tbody><tr><th>Box</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td>Conveyed Item</td><td><p>One or more Operational Exchange Items that are conveyed by the information flow from the sending Performers to receiving Performers.</p></td></tr><tr><td>Operational Exchange</td><td><p>Operational Exchange that specifies an information flow for specified conveyed items.</p><p>If you select an existing Operational Exchange from the drop-down list, Conveyed Item and Direction boxes will be filled with corresponding information automatically. You will be able to edit values of conveyed items.</p><p>The direction of the information flow won’t be editable.</p><ac:structured-macro ac:macro-id="8d1d0bf6-f972-4359-894c-7aba5727d5bf" ac:name="info" ac:schema-version="1"><ac:rich-text-body><p>Available if sending and receiving Performers are known from the wizard invocation context.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></td></tr><tr><td>Sending Performer</td><td><p>Performer that sends the specified conveyed information.</p><ac:structured-macro ac:macro-id="1121be01-02da-4a03-9cfd-593c174eff13" ac:name="info" ac:schema-version="1"><ac:rich-text-body><p>Available if a Performer is unknown from the wizard invocation context.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></td></tr><tr><td>Receiving Performer</td><td><p> Performer that receives the specified conveyed information.</p><ac:structured-macro ac:macro-id="eeb42d77-7eb4-49a3-bb3b-0c44d2bd70f7" ac:name="info" ac:schema-version="1"><ac:rich-text-body><p>Available if a Performer is unknown from the wizard invocation context.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></td></tr><tr><td> Direction</td><td><p> Direction of the information flow.<br /><ac:image ac:alt="Specifying the direction" ac:title="Specifying the direction"><ri:attachment ri:filename="realized_operational_exchange_wizard_direction.png"><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Realized Operational Exchange wizard" /></ri:attachment></ac:image></p><p>After changing the direction from the default one, the sending Performance is switched with the receiving Performance. The direction of the Operational Exchange is changed accordingly.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Add Operational Exchange to corresponding relationships</p></td><td><p>Select the check box, if you want to add the Operational Exchange to corresponding relationships existing in other related diagrams.</p></td></tr></tbody></table><table><tbody><tr><th>Button</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td><p><ac:image><ri:attachment ri:filename="[...]button.png"><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="_buttons" /></ri:attachment></ac:image>(by the <strong>Conveyed Item</strong> box)</p></td><td><p>Click to open the <strong>Select Conveyed Information</strong> dialog to select or create a conveyed item. You can specify more than one conveyed item.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p><ac:image><ri:attachment ri:filename="[...]button.png"><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="_buttons" /></ri:attachment></ac:image>(by the <strong>Sending Performer </strong>box)</p></td><td> Click to open the element Selection dialog.</td></tr><tr><td><p><ac:image><ri:attachment ri:filename="[...]button.png"><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="_buttons" /></ri:attachment></ac:image>(by the <strong>Receiving </strong><strong>Performer </strong>box)</p></td><td> Click to open the element Selection dialog.</td></tr></tbody></table></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></li><li><p>Producing and Consuming Activities specification (optional).</p><ac:structured-macro ac:macro-id="cb855e5b-1d49-429d-bd9a-fb7521c86700" ac:name="expand" ac:schema-version="1"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">How to specify Producing and Consuming Activities?</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p>This step is designed to specify Producing and Consuming Activities for the created or selected Operational Exchange. Operational Exchanges are produced and consumed by Activities acting under the Performers.</p><p><ac:image ac:alt="Specifying Producing and Consuming Activities in Realized Operational Exchange wizard" ac:title="Specifying Producing <!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575961 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01755: Realized Resource Interaction wizard

- page_id: `249575961`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575961/Realized+Resource+Interaction+wizard
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-08-10T11:45:12.583+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > Dialogs
- labels: ['realized-resource-interaction-wizard']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

The **Realized Resource Interaction** wizard provides you with the instructions to follow when adding a new Resource Interaction to:

- A Resource Interface between a pair of Resource Roles in the SV-1, SV-2 diagrams.
- A Function Edge (Function Control Flow and Function Object Flow) between a pair of Functions in the SV-4 Flows diagram.
- A Resource Message between a pair of two lifelines of Resources in the SV-10c diagram.

The **Realized Resource Interaction** wizard includes of two steps:

1. Resource Interaction creation (mandatory). How to create new or select an existing Resource Interaction?This step is designed to create a new Resource Interaction by specifying a conveyed Resource Interaction Item, both sending and receiving Resources, and a direction of a Resource Interaction. Depending on a fact, if selected Resources are known or not, requested information differs: 
- If sending and receiving Resources are unknown form the wizard invocation context, you need to specify both. 
[IMAGE alt='' src='']- If sending and receiving Resources are known, they are added to a **Realized Resource Interaction** wizard automatically. 
[IMAGE alt='' src='']BoxDescriptionConveyed ItemOne or more Resource Interaction Items that are conveyed by the information flow from the sending Resource to receiving Resource.Resource InteractionResource Interaction that specifies an information flow for specified conveyed items.If you select an existing Resource Interaction from the drop-down list, Conveyed Item and Direction boxes will be filled with corresponding information automatically. You will be able to edit values of conveyed items.The direction of the information flow won’t be editable.Available if sending and receiving Resources are known from the wizard invocation context.Sending ResourceResource that sends the specified conveyed information.Available if a Resource is unknown from the wizard invocation context.Receiving ResourceResource that receives the specified conveyed information.Available if a Resource is unknown from the wizard invocation context.DirectionDirection of the information flow. 
[IMAGE alt='' src='']After changing the direction from the default one, the sending resource will be switched with the receiving resource. The direction of the Resource Interaction will be changed accordingly.Add Resource Interaction to corresponding relationshipsSelect the check box, if you want to add the Resource Interaction to corresponding relationships existing in other related diagrams. These are the relationships that can realize the Resource Interaction:- System Connector (SV-1 Systems Interface Internal Description, SV-2 Systems Communications Internal Description)- Resource Connector (DoDAF) / Resource Interface (MODAF / NAF) (SV-1 Systems Interface Internal Description, SV-2 Systems Communications Internal Description)- Function Edge (SV-4 Systems Functionality Description)- Resource Message (SV-10c Systems Event-Trace Description)ButtonDescription[IMAGE alt='' src=''](by the **Conveyed Item** box)Click to open the element Selection dialog to select or create a conveyed item. You can specify more than one conveyed item.[IMAGE alt='' src=''](by the **Sending Resource** box)Click to open the element Selection dialog.[IMAGE alt='' src=''](by the **Receiving Resource** box)Click to open the element Selection dialog.
2. step2Producing and Consuming Functions specification (optional). Click here for detailed descriptionThis step is designed to specify Producing and Consuming Functions for the created or selected Resource Interaction. Resource Interactions are produced and consumed by Activities acting under the Resource (System Function (DoDAF) or Function (MODAF / NAF)). In terms of UPDM, Resources perform System Functions (DoDAF) or Functions (MODAF / NAF).[IMAGE alt='' src='']There should always be a pair of functions: one to produce and other to consume information flow

To open the **Realized Resource Interaction** wizard do one of the following

- Create the Resource Interaction relationship between System Resources. Click here to see the views for which this action is available**DoDAF:**[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Description' space='UPDM2P'][CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-2 Systems Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'][CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P']**MODAF:**SV-1 Resource Interaction SpecificationSV-2 Resource Communications DescriptionSV-4 Functionality Description**NAF:**NSV-1 System Interface DescriptionNSV-2 System Communications DescriptionNSV-4 System Functionality Description
- Select a Resource Connector or a Resource Interface and click [IMAGE alt='' src=''] on the smart manipulator toolbar. Click here to see the views for which this action is available**DoDAF:**[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Internal Description' space='UPDM2P'][CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-2 Systems Internal Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P']**MODAF:**SV-1 Resource Internal Interaction SpecificationSV-2 Resource Internal Communications Description
- On the diagram pallet, click [IMAGE alt='' src=''] and select a Resource Connector or a Resource Interface. Click here to see the views for which this action is available**DoDAF:**[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Internal Description' space='UPDM2P'][CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-2 Systems Internal Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P']**MODAF:**SV-1 Resource Internal Interaction SpecificationSV-2 Resource Internal Communications Description
- Select a Function Edge and click [IMAGE alt='' src=''] on the smart manipulator toolbar. Click here to see the views for which this action is available**DoDAF:**[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P']**MODAF:**SV-4 Functionality Description**NAF:**NSV-4 System Functionality Description
- In the diagram pallet, click [IMAGE alt='' src=''] and select a Function Edge. Click here to see the views for which this action is available**DoDAF:**[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P']**MODAF:**SV-4 Functionality Description**NAF:**NSV-4 System Functionality Description
- On the table toolbar, click the**Add New** button. Click here to see the views for which this action is available**DoDAF:**[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P']**MODAF:**SV-4 Functionality Description**NAF:**NSV-4 System Functionality Description
- Select a Resource Message and click [IMAGE alt='' src=''] on the smart manipulator toolbar. Click here to see the views for which this action is available**DoDAF:**[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-10c Systems Event-Trace Description' space='UPDM2P']**MODAF:**SV-10c Resource Event-Trace Description**NAF:**NSV-10c Systems Event-Trace Description
- In the diagram pallet, click [IMAGE alt='' src=''] and select a Resource Message. Click here to see the views for which this action is available**DoDAF:**[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-10c Systems Event-Trace Description' space='UPDM2P']**MODAF:**SV-10c Resource Event-Trace Description**NAF:**NSV-10c Systems Event-Trace Description

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575619 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01756: Relating Projects in Lr diagram

- page_id: `249575619`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575619/Relating+Projects+in+Lr+diagram
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-31T09:36:09.050+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > NAF 4.0 viewpoints and views > Logical viewpoint > Lr Lines of Development > Manipulations in Lr Lines of Development (Lr Gantt chart)
- labels: ['relate-project-in-lr']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

You can relate projects to a sequence using the following relation types:

- Finish to Start. Target project cannot start earlier than the source project finishes.
- Start to Start. The target project cannot start earlier than the source project starts.
- Finish to Finish. The target project cannot finish earlier than the source project finishes.
- Start to Finish. The target project cannot finish earlier than the source project starts.

You can change project dates by moving a project across the timeline. The Actual Project Sequence validation rule is executed while changing the related project dates. If dates in the project sequence violate the rule, the relation is highlighted in red.

To relate projects

1. Select two Projects.
2. On the diagram toolbar, click Relate .
3. Select one of the available relation types:
  - Finish to Start
  - Start to Start
  - Finish to Finish
  - Start to Finish

To remove the relation between projects

1. Select two related Projects.
2. On the diagram toolbar, click Relate .
3. Select None .

To resolve the incorrect project sequence

1. On the highlighted relation shortcut menu, click Validate .
2. Select one of the suggested solutions. 
[IMAGE alt='' src=''] If you change dates of a Project containing Sub Projects, the Sub Project dates change correspondingly.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html

The target project cannot finish earlier than the source project finishes.</li><li>Start to Finish. The target project cannot finish earlier than the source project starts.</li></ul><p>You can change project dates by moving a project across the timeline. If dates in the project sequence violate the rule, the relation is highlighted in red.</p><p> </p><p>To relate projects</p><hr /><ol><li>Select two Projects.</li><li>On the diagram toolbar, click <strong>Relate</strong>.</li><li>Select one of the available relation types:<br /><ul><li><strong>Finish to Start</strong></li><li><strong>Start to Start</strong></li><li><strong>Finish to Finish</strong></li><li><strong>Start to Finish</strong></li></ul></li></ol><p> </p><p>To remove the relation between projects</p><hr /><ol><li>Select two related Projects.</li><li>On the diagram toolbar, click <strong>Relate</strong>.</li><li>Select <strong>None</strong>.</li></ol><p> </p><p>To resolve the incorrect project sequence</p><hr /><ol><li>On the highlighted relation shortcut menu, click <strong>Validate</strong>.</li><li><p>Select one of the suggested solutions.<br /><ac:image><ri:attachment ri:filename="PV-2_Validation.png"><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Relating Projects in Lr diagram" /></ri:attachment></ac:image><br /><br /></p><ac:structured-macro ac:macro-id="1fb35907-6f21-414e-9f69-ae4a3c73a422" ac:name="info" ac:schema-version="1"><ac:rich-text-body><p>If you change dates of a Project containing Sub Projects, the Sub Project dates change correspondingly.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></li></ol></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell><p> </p></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section></ac:layout>

## PAGE 01758: Removing Capabilities from Cr diagram

- page_id: `249575570`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575570/Removing+Capabilities+from+Cr+diagram
- version_number: 1

- labels: ['delete-capabilities-from-chart-in-cr', 'remove-capability-from-cr']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

To delete a Capability from the chart

1. Select a Capability.
2. On the diagram toolbar, click the Delete From Chart button.

To delete a Capability from the model

1. Select a Capability.
2. On the diagram toolbar, click the Delete button.

- page_id: `249575621`

- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575621/Removing+Project+Status+from+Lr+diagram

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

To remove the Project Status

##### Description

A RequestPoint models the use of a service by a participant and defines the connection point through which a Participant makes requests and uses or consumes services.

##### Origin

##### Architecture Framework

##### Description

UPDM: A combination of physical element, energy, and data that are combined used to accomplish a task or function.

MODAF/NAF: A type of man-made object. Examples are “car”, “radio”, “fuel”, etc. (MODAF::Artifact, NAF::Artifact).

##### Architecture Framework

MODAF, NAF

##### Properties

| Property | Description |
| --- | --- |
| facilityType : String[0..*] | The type of facility that the artifact is associated with. |

506464327

506464329

506464328

##### Description

UPDM: A physical connection between two resources that implements protocols through which the source resource can transmit items to the destination resource.

MODAF/NAF: Asserts that a connection exists between two ports belonging to parts in a system composite structure model (MODAF::SystemPortConnector, NAF::SystemPortConnector).

DoDAF: NA

##### Architecture Framework

MODAF, NAF

##### Extensions

UML Connector

## PAGE 01770: Resource Constraint

- page_id: `249575880`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575880/Resource+Constraint
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:35:55.723+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > UPDM 2.1 Elements > UPDM 2.1 Systems Viewpoint Elements
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

554687045

554687047

554687046

##### Description

MODAF/NAF: A rule governing the structural or functional aspects of an implementation - this may also include constraints on OrganizationalResources that are part of an implementation.

DoDAF: The range of permissible states for an object (DoDAF::Constraint).

##### Architecture Framework

DoDAF, MODAF, NAF

##### Properties

| Property | Description |
| --- | --- |
| InformationTechnologyStandardCategory : String[*] | The information technology standard category that is associated with the resource constraint. |

##### Extensions

UML Constraint

##### Related DoDAF views

[SV-10a Systems Rules Model](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/SV-10a+Systems+Rules+Model)

##### Related MODAF views

[MODAF. SV-10a Resource Constraints Specification](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/MODAF.+SV-10a+Resource+Constraints+Specification)

##### Related NAF views

[NSV-10a Systems Rule Model](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UAFP190/NSV-10a+Systems+Rule+Model)

- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575882/Resource+Interaction

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

554790083

554790085

554790084

##### Description

UPDM: ResourceInteraction represents data that is exchanged between the resources.

MODAF/NAF: An assertion that two FunctionalResources interact. For example, data exchange between systems, conversations between people, people using systems.

DoDAF: NA

##### Architecture Framework

MODAF, NAF

##### Extensions

UML Information Flow

## PAGE 01773: Resource Interaction Manager dialog

- page_id: `249575966`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575966/Resource+Interaction+Manager+dialog
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-08-10T11:46:39.403+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > Dialogs
- labels: ['resource-interaction-manager-dialog']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

The Resource Interaction Manager dialog enables to analyze and manage the Resource Interactions data. You can edit existing Resource Interactions by adding new Resource Interaction Items, realizing or ignoring existing Resource Interactions on selected relationship, specifying producing and consuming Functions.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

To open the **Resource Interaction Manager** dialog

1. Select Resource Interface, Resource Connector, Association, Function Edge , or Resource Message in the diagram pane.
2. On the smart manipulator, click [ATTACHMENT filename='resource_interaction_manager.png'] . The Resource Interaction Manager dialog opens.

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

## PAGE 01774: Resource Interface

- page_id: `249575883`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575883/Resource+Interface
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:06:43.481+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > UPDM 2.1 Elements > UPDM 2.1 Systems Viewpoint Elements
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

554850866

554850868

554850867

##### Description

UPDM: ResourceInterface is a contractual agreement between two resources that implement protocols through which the source resource to the destination resource.

MODAF/NAF: NA

DoDAF: An overlap between Performers for the purpose of producing a Resource that is consumed by the other (DoDAF::Interface).

##### Architecture Framework

DoDAF, MODAF, NAF

##### Extensions

UML Association

##### Related MODAF views

[MODAF. SV-1 Resource Interaction Specification](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/MODAF.+SV-1+Resource+Interaction+Specification)

[MODAF. SV-2 Resource Internal Communications Description](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/MODAF.+SV-2+Resource+Internal+Communications+Description)

[MODAF. SV-3 Resource Interaction Matrix](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/MODAF.+SV-3+Resource+Interaction+Matrix)

[MODAF. SV-6 Systems Data Exchange Matrix](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/MODAF.+SV-6+Systems+Data+Exchange+Matrix)

##### Related NAF views

[NSV-1 System Interface Description](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/NSV-1+System+Interface+Description)

[NSV-2 System Communications Description](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/NSV-2+System+Communications+Description)

[NSV-6 Systems Data Exchange Matrix](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/NSV-6+Systems+Data+Exchange+Matrix)

554913425

##### Description

UPDM: Message for use in a Resource Event-Trace, implements a ResourceInteraction.

MODAF/NAF: A specification of the interactions between aspects of a Resources architecture (MODAF::ResourceInteractionSpecification, NAF::ResourceInteractionSpecification).

DoDAF: An overlap of an Activity with a Resource, in particular a consuming or producing Activity that expresses an input, output, consumption, or production Activity of the Resource (DoDAF::ActivityResourceOverlap).

MODAF/NAF: An interface (logical or physical) provided by a System. A SystemPort may implement a PortType though there is no requirement for SystemPorts to be typed (MODAF::SystemPort, NAF::SystemPort).

DoDAF: An interface (logical or physical) provided by a System (DoDAF::Port).

##### Architecture Framework

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249576049 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01783: Reusing Measurement Sets for Actual Objects

- page_id: `249576049`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249576049/Reusing+Measurement+Sets+for+Actual+Objects
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-05-25T08:31:34.672+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > Procedures > Managing Measurement Sets and Actual Measurements
- labels: ['reuse-measurement-sets-for-actual-objects']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

When creating a Node Role or Resource Role, you can quickly reuse the Measurement Sets of their type (Node or System Resource). For your convenience, the information about the recommended Actual Measurement Sets is displayed in the Specification window of an element for which you are creating the Actual Measurement Set.

You can conveniently reuse the values of Measurement Sets when creating the following actual objects:

- Node Role
- Resource Role
- Operational Activity Action
- Function Action
- Instances

When creating instances, the Actual Measurement Sets belonging to the classifier are copied automatically.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The type and behavior measurements in the Actual Object Measurements compartment are displayed *Italic*.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<ac:layout><ac:layout-section ac:type="two_right_sidebar"><ac:layout-cell><p>When creating a Node Role or Resource Role, you can quickly reuse the Measurement Sets of their type (Node or System Resource). For your convenience, the information about the recommended Actual Measurement Sets is displayed in the Specification window of an element for which you are creating the Actual Measurement Set.</p><p>You can conveniently reuse the values of Measurement Sets when creating the following actual objects:</p><ul><li><span style="color: rgb(124,127,147);"> </span>Node Role</li><li><span style="color: rgb(124,127,147);"> </span>Resource Role</li><li><span style="color: rgb(124,127,147);"> </span>Operational Activity Action</li><li>Function Action</li><li><span style="color: rgb(124,127,147);"> </span>Instances</li></ul><ac:structured-macro ac:name="info"><ac:rich-text-body><p>When creating instances, the Actual Measurement Sets belonging to the classifier are copied automatically.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p><ac:image><ri:attachment ri:filename="measurements_2.png"><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Reusing Measurement Sets for Actual Objects" /></ri:attachment></ac:image></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="info"><ac:rich-text-body><p>The type and behavior measurements in the Actual Object Measurements compartment are displayed <em>Italic</em>.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell><p> </p></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section></ac:layout>

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

1101034189

1101034191

1101034190

##### Description

MODAF/NAF: An abstract Class that is extended by OperationalConstraint (A rule governing an operational behaviour or property.) and ResourceConstraint (A rule governing the structural or functional aspects of an implementation - this may also include constraints on OrganisationalResources that are part of an implementation).

DoDAF: Rule: A principle or condition that governs behavior; a prescribed guide for conduct or action. Subtype: Constraint: The range of permissible states for an object.

Rule is abstract.

##### Architecture Framework

DoDAF, MODAF, NAF

##### Extensions

UML Constraint

##### Related DoDAF views

[OV-6a Operational Rules Model](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UAFP190/OV-6a+Operational+Rules+Model)

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575623 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01786: S1 Service Taxonomy

- page_id: `249575623`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575623/S1+Service+Taxonomy
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-05-05T10:57:56.106+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > NAF 4.0 viewpoints and views > Service viewpoint
- labels: ['s1-service-taxonomy', 's1']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The S1 Service Taxonomy view specifies a hierarchy of services. The elements in the hierarchy are service specifications (rather than service implementations), and the relationships between the elements are specializations – i.e. one service is a special type of another. The purpose of an S1 is to provide a governance structure for a Service-Oriented Architecture. Along with S3-Service Interfaces, it specifies a standard library of service specifications for an enterprise, which service implementers are expected to conform to.

A service is an implementation-independent specification of a packaged element of functionality and/or capability. There is potential for confusion between services and capabilities. The key indicator of a service is that it provides a standard interface to consumers. This means that services may be used as “wrappers” for one or more capability in order to provide a standard method of access to the capability. A well-designed service taxonomy provides a set of specifications for capability providers to adhere to. Services may have attributes and constraints (service policy) defined against them. Attributes are inherited by specialized services. Where an attribute is specified for a service, implementations of that service shall specify their values for the attribute.

The S1 view may be used to:

- SOA governance.
- Identification of services.
- Service planning.
- Service audit.
- Service gap analysis.
- Providing reference services for architectures.
- Tailoring generic services for specific applications.

**Implementation**

The S1 view can be represented using:

- A S1 Service Taxonomy diagram which is based on the UML Class diagram. [ATTACHMENT filename='S1.png']
- A C1-S1 Capability to Services Mapping matrix. [ATTACHMENT filename='S1_matrix.png']

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating S1 diagram' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating C1-S1 matrix' space='UPDM2P']

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Service Interface
- Capability
- Expose

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html

The purpose of an S1 is to provide a governance structure for a Service-Oriented Architecture. <!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575628 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01787: S3 Service Interfaces

- page_id: `249575628`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575628/S3+Service+Interfaces
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-05-05T11:01:02.194+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > NAF 4.0 viewpoints and views > Service viewpoint
- labels: ['s3-service-interfaces', 's3']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The purpose of the S3 Service Interfaces view is to define the interfaces presented by a service. A service presents one or more interfaces to consumers (a “consumer” being any agent capable of using the service – a person, an organization, a system or another service). In this case, the architect specifies provided interfaces. A service may also be capable of using interfaces exposed by other services, and the architect may specify these as used interfaces.

Specifying the interfaces that a service provides and uses defines which services are compatible with which other services. If Service A provides an interface, X and Service B can use Interface X then Service B can call upon at least some of the functionality of Service A.

**Implementation**

The S3 view can be represented using:

- A S3 Service Interfaces diagram which is based on the UML Class diagram. [ATTACHMENT filename='S3.png']
- A S3 MS Word document report.

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Service Interface
- Service Operation
- Service Attribute
- Service Parameter
- Service
- Request

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html

## PAGE 01788: S4 Service Functions

- page_id: `249575630`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575630/S4+Service+Functions
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-05-05T11:01:39.666+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > NAF 4.0 viewpoints and views > Service viewpoint
- labels: ['s4-service-functions', 's4']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The S4 Service Functions view defines the behavior of a service in terms of the functions it is expected to perform. S4 is the key behavioral specification for services. Equivalent in nature to [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='L4 Logical Activities' space='UPDM2P'] and R4 - Resource Functions, it specifies a set of functions that a service implementation is expected to perform.

**Implementation**

The S4 view can be represented using:

- A S4 Service Functions Taxonomy diagram based on the UML Clas diagram. [ATTACHMENT filename='S4.png']

- A S4 Service Functions diagram for the Operational Activity flows. This diagram is based on the UML Activity diagram. [ATTACHMENT filename='S4_service_functions.png']
- A UML Activity diagram.
- A SysML Activity diagram.
- A SysML Block Definition diagram.
- A UML Class diagram.

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating S4 Service Functions diagram' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating S4 Service Functions Taxonomy diagram' space='UPDM2P']

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Service Function
- Service Operation Action
- Service Function Action
- Function Edge
- Service Operation
- Service Parameter
- Service Interface

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575635 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01789: S5 Service States

- page_id: `249575635`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575635/S5+Service+States
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-05-05T11:02:20.489+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > NAF 4.0 viewpoints and views > Service viewpoint
- labels: ['s5-service-states', 's5']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The purpose of the S5 Service States view is to specify the possible states a service may have, and the possible transitions between those states. It is generally considered good practice to make services stateless – i.e. consumers of a service are not aware of what state the service is in. However, in specifying a service, it is often necessary to specify the allowable states so as to constrain how implementations of the service will behave. S5 is a specification of those states, and the possible transitions between them.

**Implementation**

The S5 view can be represented using a S5 Service States diagram. 
[IMAGE alt='' src='']

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Service State Machine
- Service Interface

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<ac:layout><ac:layout-section ac:type="two_right_sidebar"><ac:layout-cell><p><strong>Description</strong></p><p>The purpose of the S5 Service States view is to specify the possible states a service may have, and the possible transitions between those states. It is generally considered good practice to make services stateless – i.e. consumers of a service are not aware of what state the service is in. However, in specifying a service, it is often necessary to specify the allowable states so as to constrain how implementations of the service will behave. S5 is a specification of those states, and the possible transitions between them.</p><p><strong>Implementation</strong></p><p>The S5 view can be represented using a <ac:inline-comment-marker ac:ref="ee4b8256-c894-4fc6-aa98-222af27fda31">S5 Service States diagram</ac:inline-comment-marker>.<br /><ac:image ac:alt="S5 Service States diagram" ac:title="S5 Service States diagram"><ri:attachment ri:filename="S5.png"><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="S5 Service States" /></ri:attachment></ac:image></p></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell><p> </p></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section><ac:layout-section ac:type="two_equal"><ac:layout-cell><ac:structured-macro ac:name="panel"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Related elements</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><ul><li>Service State Machine</li><li>Service Interface</li></ul></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell><p> </p></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section></ac:layout>

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575637 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01790: S6 Service Interactions

- page_id: `249575637`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575637/S6+Service+Interactions
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-05-05T11:02:42.813+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > NAF 4.0 viewpoints and views > Service viewpoint
- labels: ['s6-service-interactions', 's6']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The purpose of S6 Service Interactions view is to specify how a service interacts with external agents, and the sequence and dependencies of those interactions. An S6 product does not specify the sequencing of an orchestrated set of services (see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='L6 Logical Sequence' space='UPDM2P']). Its purpose is to specify the general sequence of interactions that are possible for a given service.

**Implementation**

The S6 view can be represented using a S6 Service Interactions diagram which is based on the UML Sequence diagram.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Service Interaction
- Service Message
- Service Interface
- Service Attribute

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html

An S6 product does not specify the sequencing of an orchestrated set of services (see <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="L6 Logical Sequence" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[L6 - Logical Sequence]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link>). Its purpose is to specify the general sequence of interactions that are possible for a given service.</p><p><strong>Implementation</strong></p><p>The S6 view can be represented using a S6 Service Interactions diagram which is based on the UML Sequence diagram.</p><p><ac:image ac:alt="S6 Service Interactions diagram" ac:title="S6 Service Interactions diagram"><ri:attachment ri:filename="S6.png"><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="S6 Service Interactions" /></ri:attachment></ac:image></p></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell><p> </p></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section><ac:layout-section ac:type="two_equal"><ac:layout-cell><ac:structured-macro ac:name="panel"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Related elements</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><ul><li>Service Interaction</li><li>Service Message</li><li>Service Interface</li><li>Service Attribute</li></ul></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell><p> </p></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section></ac:layout>

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575639 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01791: S7 Service IF Parameters

- page_id: `249575639`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575639/S7+Service+IF+Parameters
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-10-21T07:52:52.525+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > NAF 4.0 viewpoints and views > Service viewpoint
- labels: ['s7-service-i/f-parameters', 's7']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The S7 Service I/F Parameters view identifies all the parameters used in Service Interfaces (see also [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='S3 Service Interfaces' space='UPDM2P']).

**Implementation**

The S7 view can be represented using S7 Service I/F Parameters diagram which is based on the UML Class diagram.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575641 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01792: S8 Service Policy

- page_id: `249575641`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575641/S8+Service+Policy
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-05-05T11:03:53.033+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > NAF 4.0 viewpoints and views > Service viewpoint
- labels: ['s8-service-policy', 's8']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The purpose of the S8 Service Policy view is to specify constraints that apply to implementations of services. To better enable consistency and re-use of service specifications, it is important to set constraints on how a service should behave. An S8 product specifies constraints against services to which implementations of must conform.

**Implementation**

The S8 view can be represented using:

- A S8 Service Policy table. [ATTACHMENT filename='S8.png']
- A S8 spreadsheet report .

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating S8 table' space='UPDM2P']

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Service Policy
- Service Interface

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249576002 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01796: Select Symbol dialog

- page_id: `249576002`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249576002/Select+Symbol+dialog
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-10-20T13:29:23.968+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > Dialogs
- labels: ['select-symbol-dialog', 'affiliation', 'frame']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

Use **Select Symbol** dialog to apply military symbols for resources.

To open the **Select Symbol** dialog, do either

- Create resources from MIL-STD-2525C Symbology toolbar.
- Select resource and click [ATTACHMENT filename='military_symbols.png'] on the smart manipulator toolbar.
- Open the Specification window of any UPDM element. Select Image property cell and click [ATTACHMENT filename='military_symbols.png'] . The **Select Symbol** dialog opens.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The **Select Symbol** dialog consists of these four components:

##### Whole hierarchy tree/ Recently used tree

Select the military symbol from the Whole hierarchy tree or Recently used tree.

##### Quick filter

You can search for symbols in the **Whole hierarchy** or **Recently used** tabs by using one of the following way:

- Simple Search: type what you want to find in the hierarchy.
- ID Search: use an MIL-STD-2525C symbology ID to find the exact symbol in the hierarchy. For example, type "1.X.3.2.2.1.3".
- Pattern Search: type * to find any symbols. For example, type "*Frying" if you want to find "Fixed Wing" somewhere in the hierarchy.

##### Affiliation area

Affiliation - the threat posed by the warfighting object being represented. The basic affiliation categories are unknown, friend, neutral, and hostile. Additionally the pending, suspect, assumed friend, joker and faker affiliations may be applied. Affiliation can be defined for all military symbols available. Its a bit different with a frame property. It can be changed for no more than 1/5 of a symbols.

##### Frame area

Frame - the geometric border of a symbol that provides an indication of the affiliation, battle dimension, and status of a warfighting object.

##### Preview area

You can preview the symbol before applying it on the resource.

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Applying military symbols' space='UPDM2P']

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

## PAGE 01797: Service

- page_id: `249575863`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`

- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

314459507

314459509

314459508

##### Description

A ServicePoint is the offer of a service by one participant to others using well defined terms, conditions and interfaces. A ServicePoint defines the connection point through which a Participant offers its capabilities and provides a service to clients.

##### Origin

SoaML

##### Architecture Framework

DoDAF, MODAF, NAF

##### Extensions

UML Port

##### Related DoDAF views

[SV-1 Systems Interface Description](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/SV-1+Systems+Interface+Description)

[SvcV-2 Services Resource Flow Description](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/SvcV-2+Services+Resource+Flow+Description)

[SvcV-3a Systems-Services Matrix](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/SvcV-3a+Systems-Services+Matrix)

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249576108 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01801: Service Channels Summary Matrix

- page_id: `249576108`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249576108/Service+Channels+Summary+Matrix
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-16T12:08:05.798+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > Procedures
- labels: ['service-channels-summary-matrix']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

A Service Channel Summary matrix enables a quick overview of all the service interactions specified in one or more OV and SV models. The matrix format supports a rapid assessment of potential commonalities and redundancies (or, if fault-tolerance is desired, the lack of redundancies). In addition, this model is useful in support of net-centric (service-oriented) implementation of services.

The Service Channel Summary Matrix can be organized in a number of ways to emphasize the association of service pairs in context with the architecture’s purpose. One type of organization is a Service Hierarchy or Taxonomy of Services.

The intended usage of the Service Channel Summary Matrix includes:

- Summarizing service resource interactions.
- Interface management.
- Comparing interoperability characteristics of solution options.

**Implementation**

Service Channel Summary Matrix can be represented using a Service Channel Summary Matrix diagram which is an editable Dependency Matrix.

**Sample**

**[IMAGE alt='' src='']**

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Service Channel
- Service Interface
- Service
- Request
- System
- Materiel
- Post

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249576105 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01802: Service Channels Summary Table

- page_id: `249576105`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249576105/Service+Channels+Summary+Table
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-16T12:08:26.513+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > Procedures
- labels: ['service-channels-summary-table']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The Service Channel Summary Table specifies the characteristics of service resource flows between Services. The Service Channel Summary Table is the physical equivalent of the logical OV-3 Operational Resource Flow Matrix and provides detailed information on the service connections which implement the Resource Flow exchanges specified in OV-3 Operational Resource Flow Matrix.

In addition, this model is useful in support of net-centric (service-oriented) implementation of services. According to the Net-Centric Data Strategy, a net-centric implementation needs to focus in on the data in the Service Resource Flow, as well as the services that produce or consume the data of the Service Resource Flow. In a net-centric implementation, not all the consumers are known and this model emphasizes the focus on the producer and Service Resource Flow.

**Implementation**

Service Channel Summary Table can be represented using:

- A Service Channel Summary Table diagram.
- A Service Channel Summary Table spreadsheet report.

**Sample**

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Service Channel
- Service Interface
- Service
- Request
- Expose
- Service Operation
- Service Parameter
- Performer
- System
- Materiel
- Capability Configuration
- Post

244656555

##### Description

UPDM: Package containing the elements that describe a service, from DoDAF 2.

DoDAF: Information necessary to interact with the service in such terms as the service inputs, outputs, and associated semantics. The service description also conveys what is accomplished when the service is invoked and the conditions for using the service.

##### Architecture Framework

DoDAF

##### Extensions

UML Package

## PAGE 01807: Service Interface

- page_id: `249575858`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575858/Service+Interface
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:15:40.976+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > UPDM 2.1 Elements > UPDM 2.1 Services Viewpoint and Service Oriented Viewpoint Elements
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

246531099

246531102

246531101

##### Description

UPDM: A contractual agreement between two resources that implement protocols through which the source service interacts to the destination resource. A physical connection between two resources that implements protocols through which the source resource can transmit items to the destination resource.

MODAF/NAF: The mechanism by which a Service communicates.

DoDAF: An overlap between Performers for the purpose of producing a Resource that is consumed by the other (DoDAF::Interface).

SOAML: Defines the interface to a Service Point or Request Point and is the type of a role in a service contract.

##### Architecture Framework

DoDAF, MODAF, NAF

##### Properties

| Property | Description |
| --- | --- |
| serviceInteraction : ServiceInteraction[0..1] | A Service interaction. |
| serviceStateMachine : ServiceStateMachine[0..1] | A Service state machine. |

##### Extensions

UML Class

## PAGE 01809: Service Operation

- page_id: `249575860`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575860/Service+Operation
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:11:26.101+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > UPDM 2.1 Elements > UPDM 2.1 Services Viewpoint and Service Oriented Viewpoint Elements
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

249474688

249474690

249474689

##### Description

UPDM: A ServiceOperation provides the access point for invoking the behavior of a provided service. The ServiceOperations are defined on ServiceInterfaces and mirrored on the providing Resource to handle calls forwarded on by the interface.

MODAF/NAF: A function or procedure which enables programmatic communication with a Service via a ServiceInterface (MODAF::ServiceInterfaceOperation).

##### Architecture Framework

DoDAF, MODAF, NAF

##### Properties

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| abstractBehavior : ServiceFunction[0..1] | Links a ServiceOperation to the abstract description of its behavior, as provided by a ServiceFunction. |
| concreteBehavior : Function[0..1] | Links a ServiceOperation to the concrete description of its behavior, as provided by a Function. |

##### Extensions

UML Operation

##### Related DoDAF views

[SvcV-2 Services Resource Flow Description](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/SvcV-2+Services+Resource+Flow+Description)

[SvcV-3a Systems-Services Matrix](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/SvcV-3a+Systems-Services+Matrix)

[SvcV-4 Services Functionality Description](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/SvcV-4+Services+Functionality+Description)

[SvcV-6 Services Resource Flow Matrix](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/SvcV-6+Services+Resource+Flow+Matrix)

[SvcV-10c Services Event-Trace Description](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/SvcV-10c+Services+Event-Trace+Description)

##### Related MODAF views

[MODAF. SOV-2 Service Interface Specification](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/MODAF.+SOV-2+Service+Interface+Specification)

[MODAF. SOV-5 Service Functionality Flow](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/MODAF.+SOV-5+Service+Functionality+Flow)

##### Related NAF views

[NSOV-2 Service Definitions](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/NSOV-2+Service+Definitions)

[NSOV-5 Service Behaviour Definition](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/NSOV-5+Service+Behaviour+Definition)

## PAGE 01810: Service Operation Action

- page_id: `249575861`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575861/Service+Operation+Action
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:24:55.426+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > UPDM 2.1 Elements > UPDM 2.1 Services Viewpoint and Service Oriented Viewpoint Elements
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

249789275

249789278

249789277

##### Description

UPDM Artifact: A call action that represents a Resource or Service Function invoking a ServiceOperation. This is used by a consuming Resource to model the call into the service. This concept is required for mapping the architecture with UML and does not have a DoDAF or MODAF equivalent.

##### Architecture Framework

DoDAF, MODAF, NAF

##### Extensions

UML Call Operation Action

##### Related DoDAF views

[SvcV-4 Services Functionality Description](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/SvcV-4+Services+Functionality+Description)

##### Related MODAF views

[MODAF. SOV-5 Service Functionality Flow](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/MODAF.+SOV-5+Service+Functionality+Flow)

##### Related NAF views

[NSOV-5 Service Behaviour Definition](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/NSOV-5+Service+Behaviour+Definition)
