<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575622 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01814: Service viewpoint

- page_id: `249575622`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575622/Service+viewpoint
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-05-13T10:11:38.444+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > NAF 4.0 viewpoints and views
- labels: ['service-viewpoint']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

The Service viewpoint is based on the concept of a Service-Oriented Architecture (SOA), which is fundamental to the NNEC paradigm. It is a description of services needed to directly support the operational domain as described in the[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Logical viewpoint' space='UPDM2P']. A service, within the Service viewpoint, is understood in its broadest sense, as a unit of work through which a provider provides a useful result to a consumer. It focuses strictly on identifying and describing services. The viewpoint also supports the description of service taxonomies, service orchestrations, a mapping of services to operational activities, and a description of various forms of service behavior.

#### PANEL: Views

Views

1

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575200 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01815: Services viewpoint

- page_id: `249575200`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575200/Services+viewpoint
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:42:26.233+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views
- labels: ['services-viewpoint']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

984167070

984167073

984167072

“The DoDAF-described Models within the Services Viewpoint describes services and their interconnections providing or supporting, DoD functions. DoD functions include both warfighting and business functions. The Service Models associate service resources to the operational and capability requirements. These resources support the operational activities and facilitate the exchange of information. The relationship between architectural data elements across the Services Viewpoint to the Operational Viewpoint and Capability Viewpoint can be exemplified as services are procured and fielded to support the operations and capabilities of organizations. The structural and behavioral models in the OVs and SvcVs allow architects and stakeholders to quickly ascertain which functions are carried out by humans and which by Services for each alternative specification and so carry out trade analysis based on risk, cost, reliability, etc.” [DoDAF V2.0 Volume II]

984167068

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249576051 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01816: Setting up Automatic Population of Measurement Sets

- page_id: `249576051`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249576051/Setting+up+Automatic+Population+of+Measurement+Sets
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-16T11:06:56.889+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > Procedures > Managing Measurement Sets and Actual Measurements
- labels: ['set-up-automatic-population-of-measurement-sets']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

You can set up the automatic measurementSet population each time creating the Instance of the associated type. 
 
 To set up the automatic Measurement Set population

1. Create a Measurement Set.
2. Add measurements for the created Measurement Set.
3. Apply « DoDAF Properties» stereotype to the created Measurement Set.
4. Open the Measurement Set Specification window and make sure the Expert properties mode is selected.
5. In the Tags property group, select the appliesFor and click the Create Value button.
6. Select the Exchange Element stereotype as the appliesFor tag value. [ATTACHMENT filename='exchange_element_as_the appliedFor_tag_value.png']
7. Save and reload the project.

You can see and edit your custom measurements.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

If you want to see your measurements in a separate group within Exchange Element specification, add group name to the Measurement Set documentation field.

## PAGE 01820: Standard

- page_id: `249575903`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575903/Standard
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:33:55.155+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > UPDM 2.1 Elements > UPDM 2.1 Standards Viewpoint and Technical Standards Viewpoint Elements
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

555942772

555942774

555942773

##### Description

MODAF/NAF: A ratified and peer-reviewed specification that is used to guide or constrain the architecture. A Standard may be applied to any element in the architecture via the [constrainedItem] property of UML::Constraint.

DoDAF: A formal agreement documenting generally accepted specifications or criteria for products, processes, procedures, policies, systems, and/or personnel.

##### Architecture Framework

DoDAF, MODAF, NAF

##### Properties

| Property | Description |
| --- | --- |
| InformationTechnologyStandardCategory: String[*] | The information technology standard category which the «Standard» belongs to. |
| currentStatus : String[1] | The current status of the Standard. |
| mandatedDate : ISO8601DateTime[1] | The date the version of the standard was published. |
| ratifiedBy : ActualOrganization[1] | The organization that ratified this Standard. |
| retiredDate : ISO8601DateTime[1] | The date the version of the standard was retired. |
| shortName : String[1] | The short name of the standard. |
| version : String[1] | Represents the revision number of the standard, e.g., “1.2.1”, “v2”, “:2004”, etc. |

##### Extensions

UML Class

##### Related DoDAF views

[StdV-1 Standards Profile](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/StdV-1+Standards+Profile)

[StdV-2 Standards Forecast](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/StdV-2+Standards+Forecast)

[SV-2 Systems Internal Resource Flow Description](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/SV-2+Systems+Internal+Resource+Flow+Description)

[SV-9 Systems Technology and Skills Forecast](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/SV-9+Systems+Technology+and+Skills+Forecast)

##### Related MODAF views

[MODAF. SV-2 Resource Internal Communications Description](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/MODAF.+SV-2+Resource+Internal+Communications+Description)

[MODAF. SV-9 Technology and Skills Forecast](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/MODAF.+SV-9+Technology+and+Skills+Forecast)

[MODAF. TV-1 Standards Profile](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UAFP190/MODAF.+TV-1+Standards+Profile)

[MODAF. TV-2 Standards Forecast](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/MODAF.+TV-2+Standards+Forecast)

##### Related NAF views

[NSV-2 System Communications Description](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/NSV-2+System+Communications+Description)

[NSV-9 Technology Forecast](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/NSV-9+Technology+Forecast)

[NTV-1 Technical Standards Profile](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P/NTV-1+Technical+Standards+Profile)

555985777

555985778

##### Description

## PAGE 01822: Standard Operational Activity

- page_id: `249575774`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575774/Standard+Operational+Activity
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:35:35.757+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > UPDM 2.1 Elements > UPDM 2.1 Capability Viewpoint and Strategic Viewpoint Elements
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

916761723

916761725

916761724

##### Description

MODAF/NAF: An OperationalActivity that is a standard procedure that is doctrinal.

This is equivalent to what some defense organizations call JETLs.

DoDAF: Work, not specific to a single organization, weapon system or individual, that transforms inputs into outputs or changes their state (DoDAF::Activity).

##### Architecture Framework

DoDAF, MODAF, NAF

##### Extensions

UML Activity

##### Related DoDAF views

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575318 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01823: Standards viewpoint

- page_id: `249575318`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575318/Standards+viewpoint
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-17T11:57:55.935+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views
- labels: ['standards-viewpoint']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

“The DoDAF-described Models within the Standards Viewpoint is the set of rules governing the arrangement, interaction, and interdependence of parts or elements of the Architectural Description. These sets of rules can be captured at the enterprise level and applied to each solution, while each solution’s architectural description depicts only those rules pertinent to architecture described. Its purpose is to ensure that a solution satisfies a specified set of operational or capability requirements. The Standards Models capture the doctrinal, operational, business, technical, or industry implementation guidelines upon which engineering specifications are based, common building blocks are established, and solutions are developed. It includes a collection of the doctrinal, operational, business, technical, or industry standards, implementation conventions, standards options, rules, and criteria that can be organized into profiles that govern solution elements for a given architecture. Current DoD guidance requires the Technical Standards portions of models be produced from DISR to determine the minimum set of standards and guidelines for the acquisition of all DoD systems that produce, use, or exchange information.” [DoDAF V2.0 Volume II]

#### PANEL: Views

Views

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html

These sets of rules can be captured at the enterprise level and applied to each solution, while each solution’s architectural description depicts only those rules pertinent to architecture described. Its purpose is to ensure that a solution satisfies a specified set of operational or capability requirements. The Standards Models capture the doctrinal, operational, business, technical, or industry implementation guidelines upon which engineering specifications are based, common building blocks are established, and solutions are developed. <!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575319 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01825: StdV-1 Standards Profile

- page_id: `249575319`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575319/StdV-1+Standards+Profile
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-06-11T08:25:24.772+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Standards viewpoint
- labels: ['stdv-1-standards-profile', 'stdv-1']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The StdV-1 defines the technical, operational, and business standards, guidance, and policy applicable to the architecture being described. As well as identifying applicable technical standards, the DoDAF V2.0 StdV-1 also documents the policies and standards that apply to the operational or business context. The DISR is an architecture resource for technical standards that can be used in the generation of the StdV-1 and StdV-2 Standards Forecast.

In most cases, building a Standards Profile consists of identifying and listing the applicable portions of existing and emerging documentation. A StdV-1 should identify both existing guidelines, as well as any areas lacking guidance. As with other models, each profile is assigned a specific timescale (e.g., “As-Is”, “To-Be”, or transitional). Linking the profile to a defined timescale enables the profile to consider both emerging technologies and any current technical standards that are expected to be updated or become obsolete. If more than one emerging standard time-period is applicable to an architecture, then a StdV-2 Standards Forecast should be completed as well as a StdV-1.

The intended usage of the StdV-1 includes:

- Application of standards (informing project strategy).
- Standards compliance.

**Implementation**

StdV-1 can be represented by a StdV-1 table.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The Standards cited are referenced as relationships to the systems, services, system functions, service functions, system data, service data, hardware/software items or communication protocols, where applicable, in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-2 Systems Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-6 Systems Resource Flow Matrix' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-1 Services Context Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-2 Services Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-4 Services Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-6 Services Resource Flow Matrix' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='DIV-2 Logical Data Model' space='UPDM2P'], and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='DIV-3 Physical Data Model' space='UPDM2P'].

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Functional Standard
- Technical Standard
- Protocol

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575322 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01826: StdV-2 Standards Forecast

- page_id: `249575322`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575322/StdV-2+Standards+Forecast
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T13:00:10.875+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Standards viewpoint
- labels: ['stdv-2-standards-forecast', 'stdv-2']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The StdV-2 contains expected changes in technology related standards, operational standards, or business standards and conventions, which are documented in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='StdV-1 Standards Profile' space='UPDM2P'] model. The forecast for evolutionary changes in the standards need to be correlated against the time periods mentioned in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-8 Systems Evolution Description' space='UPDM2P'].

[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-8 Systems Evolution Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-9 Systems Technology and Skills Forecast' space='UPDM2P'], and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-9 Services Technology and Skills Forecast' space='UPDM2P'] models.

A StdV-2 is a detailed description of emerging standards relevant to the systems, operational, and business activities covered by the Architectural Description. The forecast should be tailored to focus on areas that are related to the purpose for which a given Architectural Description is being built, and should identify issues that affect the architecture. A StdV-2 complements and expands on the StdV-1Standards Profile model and should be used when more than one emerging standard time-period is applicable to the architecture.

One of the prime purposes of this model is to identify critical technology standards, their fragility, and the impact of these standards on the future development and maintainability of the architecture and its constituent elements.

The intended usage of the StdV-2 includes:

- Forecasting future changes in standards (informing project strategy).

**Implementation**

The StdV-2 can be represented using a StdV-2 table.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

StdV-2 delineates the standards that potentially impact the relevant system and service elements (from [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-2 Systems Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-6 Systems Resource Flow Matrix' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-1 Services Context Description' space='UPDM2P'],[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-2 Services Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'],[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-4 Services Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-6 Systems Resource Flow Matrix' space='UPDM2P'], and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='DIV-2 Logical Data Model' space='UPDM2P']) and relates them to the time periods that are listed in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-8 Systems Evolution Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-8 Services Evolution Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-9 Systems Technology and Skills Forecast' space='UPDM2P'], and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-9 Services Technology and Skills Forecast' space='UPDM2P'].

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Functional Standard
- Technical Standard
- Protocol
- Forecast

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html

that potentially impact the relevant system and service elements (from <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="SV-1 Systems Interface Description" /></ac:link>, <ac:link><ri:page <!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575775 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01827: Structural Part

- page_id: `249575775`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575775/Structural+Part
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:19:04.346+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > UPDM 2.1 Elements > UPDM 2.1 Capability Viewpoint and Strategic Viewpoint Elements
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

917035894

917035897

917035896

##### Description

UPDM: An EnterprisePhase can be sub-divided into structural and temporal parts. StructuralPart describes the EnterprisePhase elements that describe the structure.

MODAF/NAF: Asserts that one EnterprisePhase is a spatial part of another, (MODAF::EnterpriseStructure).

This is a topological structuring relationship, hence the EnterprisePhase may be physically disjoint.

##### Architecture Framework

DoDAF, MODAF, NAF

##### Extensions

UML Property

##### Related MODAF Views

[MODAF. StV-1 Enterprise Vision](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P190/MODAF.+StV-1+Enterprise+Vision)

##### Related NAF Views

[NCV-1 Capability Vision](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/UPDM2P190/NCV-1+Capability+Vision)

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575254 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01829: SV-1 Systems Interface Description

- page_id: `249575254`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575254/SV-1+Systems+Interface+Description
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T11:44:42.414+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-1-systems-interface-description', 'sv-1']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SV-1 addresses the composition and interaction of Systems. For DoDAF V2.0, the SV-1 incorporates the human elements as types of Performers - Organizations and Personnel Types.

The SV-1 links together the operational and systems architecture models by depicting how Resources are structured and interact to realize the logical architecture specified in an OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description. A SV-1 may represent the realization of a requirement specified in an OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description (i.e., in a “To-Be” architecture), and so there may be many alternative SV models that could realize the operational requirement. Alternatively, in an “As-Is” architecture, the OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description may simply be a simplified, logical representation of the SV-1 to allow communication of key Resource Flows to non-technical stakeholders.

A System Resource Flow is a simplified representation of a pathway or network pattern, usually depicted graphically as a connector (i.e., a line with possible amplifying information). The SV-1 depicts all System Resource Flows between Systems that are of interest. Note that Resource Flows between Systems may be further specified in detail in SV-2 Systems Resource Flow Description and SV-6 Systems Resource Flow Matrix.

Sub-System assemblies may be identified in SV-1 to any level (i.e., depth) of decomposition the architect sees fit. SV-1 may also identify the Physical Assets (e.g., Platforms) at which Resources are deployed, and optionally overlay Operational Activities and Locations that utilize those Resources. In many cases, an operational activity and locations depicted in an OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description model may well be the logical representation of the resource that is shown in SV-1.

The intended usage of the SV-1 includes:

- Definition of System concepts.
- Definition of System options.
- System Resource Flow requirements capture.
- Capability integration planning.
- System integration management.
- Operational planning (capability and performer definition).

The SV-1 is used in two complementary ways:

- Describe the Resource Flows exchanged between resources in the architecture.
- Describe a solution, or solution option, in terms of the components of capability and their physical integration on platforms and other facilities.

**Implementation**

SV-1 can be represented using:

- A SV-1 diagram which is based on the UML Class diagram.
- A SV-1 diagram which is based on the UML Composite Structure diagram.
- A UML Class diagram.
- A UML Composite Structure diagram.
- A SysML Block Definition diagram.
- A SysML Internal Block diagram.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

An SV-1 can optionally be adorned with performers originally specified in an [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P']. In this way, traceability can be established from the logical OV structure to the physical SV structure.

An interaction, as depicted in the SV-1, is an indicator that information passes from one performer to another. In the case of systems, this can be expanded into further detail in an [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-2 Systems Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P']. Resource Flows are summarized in a Systems-Systems Matrix ([CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-3 Systems-Systems Matrix' space='UPDM2P']).

The System Functions performed by the Performers are specified in an [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'], but may optionally be overlaid in the SV-1.

An Operational View (OV) suite may specify a set of requirements – either as a specific operational plan, or a scenario for procurement. As [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'] and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-5 Operational Activity Model' space='UPDM2P'] specify the logical structure and behavior, SV-1 and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P']specify the physical structure and behavior (to the level of detail required by the architectural stakeholders).

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating SV-1 diagram' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating Resource Interaction in SV-1 diagram' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Applying military symbols' space='UPDM2P']

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- System
- Software
- Capability Configuration
- Organization Type
- Person Type
- Resource Port
- Resource Role
- Resource Interface
- Capability
- Capability Of Performer
- Resource Interaction
- Exchange Element
- Energy
- Geo Political Extent Type
- Performer
- Fielded Capability
- Service
- Request

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

## PAGE 01830: SV-1 Systems Interface Internal Description

- page_id: `249575258`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575258/SV-1+Systems+Interface+Internal+Description
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T12:16:10.218+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-1-systems-interface-internal-description', 'sv-1-internal']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SV-1 addresses the internal composition and interaction of Systems.

**Implementation**

SV-1 can be represented using:

- A SV-1 diagram which is based on the UML Class diagram.
- A SV-1 diagram which is based on the UML Composite Structure diagram.
- A UML Class diagram.
- A UML Composite Structure diagram.
- A SysML Block Definition diagram.
- A SysML Internal Block diagram.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

An SV-1 can optionally be adorned with performers originally specified in an [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P']. In this way, traceability can be established from the logical OV structure to the physical SV structure.

An interaction, as depicted in the SV-1, is an indicator that information passes from one performer to another. In the case of systems, this can be expanded into further detail in an [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-2 Systems Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P']. Resource Flows are summarized in a Systems-Systems Matrix ([CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-3 Systems-Systems Matrix' space='UPDM2P']).

The System Functions performed by the Performers are specified in an [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'], but may optionally be overlaid in the SV-1.

An Operational View (OV) suite may specify a set of requirements – either as a specific operational plan, or a scenario for procurement. As [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'] and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-5 Operational Activity Model' space='UPDM2P'] specify the logical structure and behavior, SV-1 and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'] specify the physical structure and behavior (to the level of detail required by the architectural stakeholders).

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575309 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01831: SV-10a Systems Rules Model

- page_id: `249575309`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575309/SV-10a+Systems+Rules+Model
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-06-11T07:57:11.804+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-10a-systems-rules-model', 'sv-10a']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SV-10a specifies functional and nonfunctional constraints on the implementation aspects of the architecture (i.e., the structural and behavioral elements of the Systems Viewpoint).

The SV-10a DoDAF-described Model describes constraints on the resources, functions, data, and ports that make up the SV. The constraints are specified in text and may be functional or structural (i.e., non-functional).

The intended usage of the SV-10a includes:

- Definition of implementation logic.
- Identification of resource constraints.

Implementation

SV-10a can be represented using:

- A SV-10a table.
- A SV-10a spreadsheet report.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

In contrast to the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-6a Operational Rules Model' space='UPDM2P'], SV-10a focuses on physical and data constraints rather than business rules.

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Resource Constraint
- System
- Software
- Capability Configuration
- Organization Type
- Person Type
- Function
- Entity Item
- Resource Interaction
- Exchange Element

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575312 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01832: SV-10b Systems State Transition Description

- page_id: `249575312`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575312/SV-10b+Systems+State+Transition+Description
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T12:55:21.565+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-10b-systems-state-transition-description', 'sv-10b']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SV-10b is a graphical method of describing a resource (or system function) response to various events by changing its state. The diagram basically represents the sets of events to which the resources in the Activities respond (by taking an action to move to a new state) as a function of its current state. Each transition specifies an event and an action.

The explicit time sequencing of service functions in response to external and internal events is not fully expressed in SV-4 Systems Functionality Description. The SV-10b can be used to describe the explicit sequencing of the functions. Alternatively, SV-10b can be used to reflect explicit sequencing of the actions internal to a single function, or the sequencing of system functions with respect to a specific resource.

The intended usage of the SV-10b includes:

- Definition of states, events and state transitions (behavioral modeling).
- Identification of constraints.

**Implementation**

SV-10b can be represented using a UML State Machine diagram.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The SV-10b can be used to describe the detailed sequencing of functions described in SV-4 Systems Functionality Description. However, the relationship between the actions included in SV-10b and the functions in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'] depends on the purposes of the architecture and the level of abstraction used in the models. The explicit sequencing of functions in response to external and internal events is not fully expressed in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P']. SV-10b can be used to reflect explicit sequencing of the functions, the sequencing of actions internal to a single function, or the sequencing of functions with respect to a specific resource.

Depending upon the architecture project’s needs, the SV-10b may be used separately or in conjunction with the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-10c Systems Event-Trace Description' space='UPDM2P'].

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Resources State Machine
- Resource State
- System
- Software
- Capability Configuration
- Organization Type
- Person Type

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575314 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01833: SV-10c Systems Event-Trace Description

- page_id: `249575314`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575314/SV-10c+Systems+Event-Trace+Description
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-06-11T08:11:40.814+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-10c-systems-event-trace-description', 'sv-10c']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SV-10c provides a time-ordered examination of the interactions between functional resources. Each event-trace diagram should have an accompanying description that defines the particular scenario or situation.

The SV-10c is valuable for moving to the next level of detail from the initial solution design, to help define a sequence of functions and system data interfaces, and to ensure that each participating resource or System Port role has the necessary information it needs, at the right time, to perform its assigned functionality.

The intended usage of the SV-10c includes:

- Analysis of resource events impacting operation.
- Behavioral analysis.
- Identification of non-functional system requirements.

**Implementation**

SV-10b can be represented using a UML State Machine diagram.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The SV-10c is typically used in conjunction with the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-10b Systems State Transition Description' space='UPDM2P'] to describe the dynamic behavior of resources. The data content of messages that connect Resource Flows in a SV-10c may be related with Resource Flows (the interactions in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Description' space='UPDM2P'] and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-3 Systems-Systems Matrix' space='UPDM2P']), Resource Flows (the data in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'] and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-6 Systems Resource Flow Matrix' space='UPDM2P']) and entities (in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='DIV-3 Physical Data Model' space='UPDM2P']) modeled in other models.

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Resource Event Trace
- Resource Message
- Resource Interaction

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<ac:layout><ac:layout-section ac:type="two_right_sidebar"><ac:layout-cell><p><strong>Description</strong></p><p>The SV-10c provides a time-ordered examination of the interactions between functional resources. <!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575317 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01834: SV-10c Systems Event-Trace Description BPD

- page_id: `249575317`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575317/SV-10c+Systems+Event-Trace+Description+BPD
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2020-06-08T13:32:43.580+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

SV-10c Systems Event-Trace Description (BPD) diagram is based on BPMN Process Diagram (BPD). It describes a sequence or flow of activities in an organization that shows how the businesswork. The diagram shows activities, events, and data that trigger or feed businessactivities.

SV-10c Systems Event-Trace Description (BPD) diagram is similar to the BPMN Process Diagram (BPD).

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<ac:layout><ac:layout-section ac:type="two_right_sidebar"><ac:layout-cell><p>SV-10c Systems Event-Trace Description (BPD) diagram is based on BPMN Process Diagram (BPD). It describes a sequence or flow of activities in an organization that shows how the <span style="color: rgb(51,51,51);">business </span>work. The diagram shows activities, events, and data that trigger or feed <span style="color: rgb(51,51,51);">business </span>activities.</p><p>SV-10c Systems Event-Trace Description (BPD) diagram is similar to the BPMN Process Diagram (BPD).</p></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell><p> </p></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section></ac:layout>
````

## PAGE 01835: SV-2 Systems Internal Resource Flow Description

- page_id: `249575265`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575265/SV-2+Systems+Internal+Resource+Flow+Description
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T12:23:29.988+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-2-systems-internal-resource-flow-description', 'sv-2-internal']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

A SV-2 specifies the internal System Resource Flows between Systems and may also list the protocol stacks used in connections.

**Implementation**

SV-2 can be represented using:

- A SV-2 diagram which is based on the UML Class diagram.
- A SV-2 diagram which is based on the UML Composite Structure diagram.
- A UM L Class diagram.
- A UML Composite Structure diagram.
- A SysML Block Definition diagram.
- A SysML Internal Block diagram.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

Any protocol referred to in a SV-2 diagram needs to be defined in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='StdV-1 Standards Profile' space='UPDM2P'].

- Resource Interface
- Resource Connector
- Resource Port
- Property

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575262 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01836: SV-2 Systems Resource Flow Description

- page_id: `249575262`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575262/SV-2+Systems+Resource+Flow+Description
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T12:23:50.294+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-2-systems-resource-flow-description', 'sv-2']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

A SV-2 specifies the System Resource Flows between Systems and may also list the protocol stacks used in connections.

A SV-2 DoDAF-described Model is used to give a precise specification of a connection between Systems. This may be an existing connection, or a specification for a connection that is to be made.

The intended usage of the SV-2 includes:

- Resource Flow specification.

**Implementation**

SV-2 can be represented using:

- A SV-2 diagram which is based on the UML Class diagram.
- A SV-2 diagram which is based on the UML Composite Structure diagram.
- A UM L Class diagram.
- A UML Composite Structure diagram.
- A SysML Block Definition diagram.
- A SysML Internal Block diagram.

Any protocol referred to in a SV-2 diagram needs to be defined in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='StdV-1 Standards Profile' space='UPDM2P'].

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating SV-2 diagram' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating Resource Interaction in SV-2 diagram' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Applying military symbols' space='UPDM2P']

- Software
- Capability Configuration
- Organization Type
- Person Type
- Resource Port
- Resource Connector
- Resource Role
- Resource Interface
- Protocol
- Functional Standard
- Technical Standard
- Service
- Request
- Energy
- Resource Interaction
- Exchange Element
- Geo Political Extent Type

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575269 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01837: SV-3 Systems-Systems Matrix

- page_id: `249575269`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575269/SV-3+Systems-Systems+Matrix
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T12:26:12.967+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-3-systems-systems-matrix', 'sv-3']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

A SV-3 enables a quick overview of all the system resource interactions specified in one or more [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Description' space='UPDM2P'] models. The SV-3 provides a tabular summary of the system interactions specified in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Description' space='UPDM2P'] model for the Architectural Description. The matrix format supports a rapid assessment of potential commonalities and redundancies (or, if fault-tolerance is desired, the lack of redundancies).

The SV-3 can be organized in a number of ways to emphasize the association of groups of system pairs in context with the architecture’s purpose.

The intended usage of the SV-3 includes:

- Summarizing system resource interactions.
- Interface management.
- Comparing interoperability characteristics of solution options.

**Implementation**

SV-3 can be represented using a SV-3 diagram which is an editable Dependency Matrix. The SV-3 matrix consists of as much rows and columns as there are Systems in the matrix data source.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Description' space='UPDM2P'] concentrates on System resources and their interactions, and these are summarized in a SV-3.

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- System
- Software
- Capability Configuration
- Organization Type
- Person Type
- Resource Interaction
- Exchange Element
- Energy
- Geo Political Extent Type

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<ac:layout><ac:layout-section ac:type="two_right_sidebar"><ac:layout-cell><p><strong>Description</strong></p><p>A SV-3 enables a quick overview of all the system resource interactions specified in one or more <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="SV-1 Systems Interface Description" /></ac:link> models. The SV-3 provides a tabular summary of the system interactions specified in the <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="SV-1 Systems Interface Description" /></ac:link> model for the Architectural Description. The matrix format supports a rapid assessment of potential commonalities and redundancies (or, if fault-tolerance is desired, the lack of redundancies).</p><p>The SV-3 can be organized in a number of ways to emphasize the association of groups of system pairs in context with the architecture’s purpose.</p><p>The intended usage of the SV-3 includes:</p><ul><li>Summarizing system resource interactions.</li><li>Interface management.</li><li>Comparing interoperability characteristics of solution options.</li></ul><p><strong>Implementation</strong></p><p>SV-3 can be represented using a SV-3 diagram which is an editable Dependency Matrix. The SV-3 matrix consists of as much rows and columns as there are Systems in the matrix data source.</p><p><ac:image ac:alt="SV-3 Systems-Systems Matrix" ac:title="SV-3 Systems-Systems Matrix"><ri:attachment ri:filename="SV-3_sys_sys_matrix.png"><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="SV-3 Systems-Systems Matrix" /></ri:attachment></ac:image></p><p>The <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="SV-1 Systems Interface Description" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[SV-1]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link> concentrates on System resources and their interactions, and these are summarized in a SV-3.</p></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell><ac:structured-macro ac:macro-id="523c1e18-c73c-4063-9d04-dbebaca9cb45" ac:name="panel" ac:schema-version="1"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Related procedures</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><ac:structured-macro ac:macro-id="53c68759-8d6c-4769-9627-66e017a7b6ea" ac:name="children" ac:schema-version="1" /></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p> </p><p> </p></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section><ac:layout-section ac:type="two_equal"><ac:layout-cell><ac:structured-macro ac:macro-id="cdc42bb8-97bf-476b-8793-0968176d2e58" ac:name="panel" ac:schema-version="1"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Related elements</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><ul><li>System</li><li>Software</li><li>Capability Configuration</li><li>Organization Type</li><li>Person Type</li><li>Resource Interaction</li><li>Exchange Element</li><li>Energy</li><li>Geo Political Extent Type</li></ul></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell><p> </p></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section></ac:layout>
````

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575279 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01838: SV-4 Functionality Description BPD

- page_id: `249575279`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575279/SV-4+Functionality+Description+BPD
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2018-07-12T10:22:41.718+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

SV-4 Functionality Description BPD (BPD) diagram is based on BPMN Process Diagram (BPD). It describes a sequence or flow of activities in an organization that shows how the businesswork. The diagram shows activities, events, and data that trigger or feed businessactivities.

SV-4 Functionality Description BPD (BPD) diagram is similar to the BPMN Process Diagram (BPD).

Some diagram elements have both UPDM and BPMN stereotypes.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<ac:layout><ac:layout-section ac:type="two_right_sidebar"><ac:layout-cell><p>SV-4 Functionality Description BPD (BPD) diagram is based on BPMN Process Diagram (BPD). It describes a sequence or flow of activities in an organization that shows how the <span style="color: rgb(51,51,51);">business </span>work. The diagram shows activities, events, and data that trigger or feed <span style="color: rgb(51,51,51);">business </span>activities.</p><p>SV-4 Functionality Description BPD (BPD) diagram is similar to the BPMN Process Diagram (BPD).</p><p>Some diagram elements have both UPDM and BPMN stereotypes.</p></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell><p> </p></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section></ac:layout>

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575273 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01839: SV-4 Systems Functionality Description

- page_id: `249575273`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575273/SV-4+Systems+Functionality+Description
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T12:29:43.819+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-4-systems-functionality-description', 'sv-4']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SV-4 addresses human and system functionality.

The primary purposes of SV-4 are to:

- Develop a clear description of the necessary data flows that are input (consumed) by and output (produced) by each resource.
- Ensure that the functional connectivity is complete (i.e., that a resource’s required inputs are all satisfied).
- Ensure that the functional decomposition reaches an appropriate level of detail.

The Systems Functionality Description provides detailed information regarding the:

- Allocation of functions to resources.
- Flow of resources between functions.

The SV-4 is the Systems Viewpoint model counterpart to the OV-5b Activity Model of the Operational Viewpoint.

The intended usage of the SV-4 includes:

- Description of task workflow.
- Identification of functional system requirements.
- Functional decomposition of systems.
- Relate human and system functions.

**Implementation**

SV-4 can be represented using:

- A SV-4 diagram for System Function hierarchies. This diagram is based on the UML Class diagram. [ATTACHMENT filename='SV-4_hierarchy.png']
- An SV-4 diagram for System Function flows. This diagram is based on the UML Activity diagram. [ATTACHMENT filename='SV-4_flows.png']
- A UML Class diagram.
- A UML Activity diagram.
- A SysML Block diagram.
- A SysML Activity diagram.

The SV-4 is the behavioral counterpart to the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Description' space='UPDM2P'] (in the same way that [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-5 Operational Activity Model' space='UPDM2P']OV-5b Operational Activity Model is the behavioral counterpart to [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P']OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description).

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Applying military symbols' space='UPDM2P']

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Function
- System
- Software
- Capability Configuration
- Organization Type
- Person Type
- Activity Performed By Performer
- Function Action
- Function Edge
- Resource Parameter
- Resource Interaction
- Exchange Element
- Energy
- Geo Political Extent Type

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575280 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01840: SV-5a Operational Activity to Systems Function Traceability Matrix

- page_id: `249575280`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575280/SV-5a+Operational+Activity+to+Systems+Function+Traceability+Matrix
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T12:35:31.556+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-5a', 'sv-5a-operational-activity-to-systems-function-traceability-matrix']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SV-5a addresses the linkage between System Functions described in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'] and Operational Activities specified in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-5 Operational Activity Model' space='UPDM2P'] or [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-5 Operational Activity Model' space='UPDM2P']. The SV-5a depicts the mapping of system functions and, optionally, the capabilities and performers that provide them to operational activities. The SV-5a identifies the transformation of an operational need into a purposeful action performed by a system or solution.

During requirements definition, the SV-5a plays a particularly important role in tracing the architectural elements associated with system function requirements to those associated with user requirements.

The intended usage of the SV-5a includes:

- Tracing functional system requirements to user requirements.
- Tracing solution options to requirements.
- Identification of overlaps or gaps.

**Implementation**

SV-5a can be represented using a SV-5a diagram which is an editable Dependency Matrix. System Functions are used as row elements and Operational Activities are used as column elements.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

DoDAF uses the term Operational Activity in the OVs and the term System Function in the SVs to refer to essentially the same kind of thing; both activities and functions are tasks that are performed, accept inputs, and develop outputs. The distinction between an Operational Activity and a Function is a question of what and how.

The Operational Activity is a specification of what is to be done, regardless of the mechanism used. A System Function is specifies how a resource carries it out. For this reason, SV-5a is a significant model, as it ties together the logical specification in the OV-5a with the physical specification of the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-4 Systems Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P']. System Functions can be carried out by Functional Resources (systems, performers executing activities, and performers).

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Function
- Operational Activity
- Implements

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

## PAGE 01841: SV-5b Operational Activity to Systems Traceability Matrix

- page_id: `249575283`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575283/SV-5b+Operational+Activity+to+Systems+Traceability+Matrix
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T12:38:29.940+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-5b-operational-activity-to-systems-traceability-matrix', 'sv-5b']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SV-5b addresses the linkage between described in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Description' space='UPDM2P'] and Operational Activities specified in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-5 Operational Activity Model' space='UPDM2P'] or [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-5 Operational Activity Model' space='UPDM2P']. The SV-5b depicts the mapping of systems and, optionally, the capabilities and performers that provide them to operational activities. The SV-5b identifies the transformation of an operational need into a purposeful action performed by a system or solution.

During requirements definition, the SV-5b plays a particularly important role in tracing the architectural elements associated with system requirements to those associated with user requirements.

The intended usage of the SV-5b includes:

- Tracing system requirements to user requirements.
- Tracing solution options to requirements.
- Identification of overlaps or gaps.

**Implementation**

SV-5b can be represented using a SV-5b diagram which is a non-editable Dependency Matrix. Systems are used as row elements and Operational Activities are used as column elements.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The SV-5b is generally presented as a matrix of the relationship between systems and activities and can be a summary of the Operational Activity to System Function Traceability Matrix ([CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-5a Operational Activity to Systems Function Traceability Matrix' space='UPDM2P']). The SV-5b can show requirements traceability with Operational Activities on one axis of a matrix, the System Functions on the other axis, and with an X, date, or phase in the intersecting cells, where appropriate.

- Operational Activity
- Activity Performed By Performer
- Implements

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575286 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01842: SV-6 Systems Resource Flow Matrix

- page_id: `249575286`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575286/SV-6+Systems+Resource+Flow+Matrix
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-06-11T07:19:17.531+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-6-systems-resource-flow-matrix', 'sv-6']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SV-6 specifies the characteristics of the System Resource Flows exchanged between systems with emphasis on resources crossing the system boundary.

The SV-6 focuses on the specific aspects of the system Resource Flow and the system Resource Flow content in a tabular format.

The intended usage of the SV-6 includes:

- Detailed definition of Resource Flows.

**Implementation**

SV-6 can be represented using:

- A SV-6 table.
- An SV-6 role-based table. A role-based table represents exchanges between Resource Roles (resource usages).
- A SV-6 spreadsheet report.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The SV-6 is the physical equivalent of the logical [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-3 Operational Resource Flow Matrix' space='UPDM2P'] table and provides detailed information on the system connections which implement the Resource Flow exchanges specified in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-3 Operational Resource Flow Matrix' space='UPDM2P'].

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating SV-6 table' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Displaying Custom Measurements' space='UPDM2P']

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- System
- Software
- Capability Configuration
- Organization Type
- Person Type
- Resource Interaction
- Exchange Element
- Energy
- Geo Political Extent Type
- Function

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575289 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01843: SV-7 Systems Measures Matrix

- page_id: `249575289`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575289/SV-7+Systems+Measures+Matrix
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-06-16T14:12:25.848+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-7-systems-measures-matrix', 'sv-7', 'sv-7-actual-measures-table', 'sv-7-typical-measures-table']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SV-7 depicts the measures (metrics) of resources. The Systems Measures Matrix expands on the information presented in a SV-1 by depicting the characteristics of the resources in the SV-1.

The intended usage of the SV-7 includes:

- Definition of performance characteristics and measures (metrics).
- Identification of non-functional requirements.

**Implementation**

SV-7 can be represented using:

- A SV-7 typical measures table. [ATTACHMENT filename='SV-7_sys_typical_mea_matrix.png']
- A SV-7 actual measures table. [ATTACHMENT filename='SvcV-7_Actual.PNG']
- A SV-7 actual measures spreadsheet report.

The Systems Measures Matrix expands on the information presented in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Description' space='UPDM2P'] by depicting the characteristics of the Systems and other Resources shown in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Description' space='UPDM2P']. The Systems Measures Matrix expands on the information presented in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-2 Systems Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'] by depicting the characteristics of the Systems shown in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-2 Systems Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'].

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating SV-7 Typical table' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating SV-7 Actual table' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Generating SV-7 Actual table from SV-7 Typical table' space='UPDM2P']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Generating document based reports' space='UPDM2P']

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- System
- Software
- Capability Configuration
- Organization Type
- Person Type
- Measure Type
- Measure
- Measurement
- Actual Property

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575295 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01844: SV-8 Systems Evolution Description

- page_id: `249575295`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575295/SV-8+Systems+Evolution+Description
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-17T08:40:37.543+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-8-systems-evolution-description', 'sv-8']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SV-8 presents a whole lifecycle view of resources (systems), describing how they change over time. It shows the structure of several resources mapped against a timeline.

The intended usage of the SV-8 includes:

- Development of incremental acquisition strategy.
- Planning technology insertion.

**Implementation**

The SV-8 view can be represented using a SV-8 Systems Evolution Description diagram which is realized as a time based diagram.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The SV-8 model shows the structure of resources modeled in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-1 Systems Interface Description' space='UPDM2P']. The changes depicted in the SV-8 are derived from the project milestones that are shown in a [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='PV-2 Project Timelines' space='UPDM2P']. When the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='PV-2 Project Timelines' space='UPDM2P'] is used for capability acquisition projects, there is likely to be a close relationship between these two models.

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Whole Life Configuration
- Version Of Configuration
- System
- Software
- Capability Configuration
- Organization Type
- Person Type
- Actual Project Milestone
- Increment Milestone
- Out Of Service Milestone

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575306 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01845: SV-9 Systems Technology and Skills Forecast

- page_id: `249575306`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575306/SV-9+Systems+Technology+and+Skills+Forecast
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T12:52:14.486+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Systems viewpoint
- labels: ['sv-9-systems-technology-and-skills-forecast', 'sv-9']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SV-9 defines the underlying current and expected supporting technologies and skills. Expected supporting technologies and skills are those that can be reasonably forecast given the current state of technology and skills as well as the expected improvements or trends. New technologies and skills are tied to specific time periods, which can correlate against the time periods used in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SV-8 Systems Evolution Description' space='UPDM2P'] milestones and linked to Capability Phases.

The SV-9 provides a summary of emerging technologies and skills that impact the architecture.

The SV-9 provides descriptions of relevant:

- Emerging capabilities.
- Industry trends.
- Predictions (with associated confidence factors) of the availability and readiness of specific hardware and software systems.
- Current and possible future skills.

In addition to providing an inventory of trends, capabilities and systems, the DoDAF-described Model SV-9 also includes an assessment of the potential impact of these items on the architecture. Given the future-oriented nature of this model, forecasts are typically made in short, mid and long-term timeframes, such as 6, 12 and 18-month intervals.

The intended usage of the SV-9 includes:

- Forecasting technology readiness against time.
- HR Trends Analysis.
- Recruitment Planning.
- Planning technology insertion.
- Input to options analysis.

**Implementation**

SV-9 can be represented using a SV-9 table.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The SV-9 DoDAF-described Model forecasts relates to the Standards Profile ([CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='StdV-1 Standards Profile' space='UPDM2P']) in that a timed forecast may contribute to the decision to retire or phase out the use of a certain standard in connection with a resource. Similarly, SV-9 forecasts relate to the Standards Forecasts ([CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='StdV-2 Standards Forecast' space='UPDM2P']) in that a certain standard may be adopted depending on a certain technology or skill becoming available (e.g., the availability of Java Script may influence the decision to adopt a new HTML standard).

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Forecast
- System
- Software
- Capability Configuration
- Organization Type
- Person Type
- Protocol
- Standard

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575210 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01846: SvcV-1 Services Context Description

- page_id: `249575210`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575210/SvcV-1+Services+Context+Description
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:17:47.285+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Services viewpoint
- labels: ['svcv-1-services-context-description', 'svcv-1']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

984445829

984445832

984445830

**Description**

The SvcV-1 addresses the composition and interaction of Services. For DoDAF V2.0, SvcV-1 incorporates human elements as types of Performers - Organizations and Personnel Types.

The SvcV-1 links together the operational and services architecture models by depicting how resources are structured and interact to realize the logical architecture specified in an OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description. A SvcV-1 may represent the realization of a requirement specified in an [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'] (i.e., in a “To-Be” Architectural Description), and so there may be many alternative SvcV models that could realize the operational requirement. Alternatively, in an “As-Is” Architectural Description, the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'] may simply be a simplified, logical representation of the SvcV-1 to allow communication of key Resource Flows to non-technical stakeholders.

The intended usage of the SvcV-1 includes:

- Definition of service concepts.
- Definition of service options.
- Service Resource Flow requirements capture.
- Capability integration planning.
- Service integration management.
- Operational planning (capability and performer definition).

The SvcV-1 is used in two complementary ways:

- Describe the Resource Flows exchanged between resources in the architecture.
- Describe a solution, or solution option, in terms of the components of capability and their physical integration on platforms and other facilities.

**Implementation**

SvcV-1 can be represented using a SvcV-1 diagram which is based on the UML class diagram.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The SvcV-1 links together the operational and services architecture models by depicting how resources are structured and interact to realize the logical architecture specified in an [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P']. A SvcV-1 may represent the realization of a requirement specified in an [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'] (i.e., in a “To-Be” Architectural Description), and so there may be many alternative SvcV models that could realize the operational requirement. Alternatively, in annus-Is” Architectural Description, the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'] may simply be a simplified, logical representation of the SvcV-1 to allow communication of key Resource Flows to non-technical stakeholders.

Some Resources can carry out service functions (activities) as described in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-4 Services Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'] models and these functions can optionally be overlaid on a SvcV-1.

The SvcV-1 depicts all Resource Flows between resources that are of interest. Note that Resource Flows between resources may be further specified in detail in the[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-2 Services Resource Flow Description' space='UPDM2P'] model and the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-6 Services Resource Flow Matrix' space='UPDM2P'].

984445828

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

A SvcV-1 may represent the realization of a requirement specified in an <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description" /></ac:link> (i.e., in a “To-Be” Architectural Description), and so there may be many alternative SvcV models that could realize the operational requirement. Alternatively, in an “As-Is” Architectural Description, the <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description" /></ac:link> may simply be a simplified, logical representation of the SvcV-1 to allow communication of key Resource Flows to non-technical stakeholders.</p><p>The intended usage of the SvcV-1 includes:</p><ul><li>Definition of service concepts.</li><li>Definition of service options.</li><li>Service Resource Flow requirements capture.</li><li>Capability integration planning.</li><li>Service integration management.</li><li>Operational planning (capability and performer definition).</li></ul><p>The SvcV-1 is used in two complementary ways:</p><ul><li>Describe the Resource Flows exchanged between resources in the architecture.</li><li>Describe a solution, or solution option, in terms of the components of capability and their physical integration on platforms and other facilities.</li></ul><p><strong>Implementation</strong></p><p>SvcV-1 can be represented using a SvcV-1 diagram which is based on the UML class diagram.</p><p><ac:image ac:align="center"><ri:attachment ri:filename="SvcV-1.png"><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="SvcV-1 Services Context Description" /></ri:attachment></ac:image></p><p>The SvcV-1 links together the operational and services architecture models by depicting how resources are structured and interact to realize the logical architecture specified in an <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description" /></ac:link>. A SvcV-1 may represent the realization of a requirement specified in an <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description" /></ac:link> (i.e., in a “To-Be” Architectural Description), and so there may be many alternative SvcV models that could realize the operational requirement. Alternatively, in annus-Is” Architectural Description, the <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="OV-2 Operational Resource Flow Description" /></ac:link> may simply be a simplified, logical representation of the SvcV-1 to allow communication of key Resource Flows to non-technical stakeholders.</p><p>Some Resources can carry out service functions (activities) as described in <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="SvcV-4 Services Functionality Description" /></ac:link> models and these functions can optionally be overlaid on a SvcV-1.</p><p>The SvcV-1 depicts all Resource Flows between resources that are of interest. Note that Resource Flows between resources may be further specified in detail in the<ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="SvcV-2 Services Resource Flow Description" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[ SvcV-2 Services Resource Flow Description]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link> model and the <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="SvcV-6 Services Resource Flow Matrix" /></ac:link>.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ac:structured-macro ac:name="content-block" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="326ed115-caae-4345-b202-e3b3b2478b15"><ac:parameter ac:name="id">984445828</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p class="auto-cursor-target"><strong>Related Pages:</strong></p><p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="children" ac:schema-version="2" ac:macro-id="4cbf182b-1332-4d43-a4b9-de9b21f0f6e7" /></p><ul><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Service Access" /></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Capability" /></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Capability of Performer" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Capability Of Performer]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Function" /></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Activity Performed By Performer" /></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Resource Interaction" /></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Resource Port" /></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="Resource Role" /></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" ri:content-title="System" /></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="UPDM2P" <!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575201 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01847: SvcV-10a Services Rules Model

- page_id: `249575201`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575201/SvcV-10a+Services+Rules+Model
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-06-18T10:49:53.560+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Services viewpoint
- labels: ['svcv-10a-services-rules-model', 'svcv-10a']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SvcV-10a is to specify functional and nonfunctional constraints on the implementation aspects of the architecture (that is, the structural and behavioral elements of the Services Model).

The SvcV-10a describes constraints on the resources, functions, data and ports that make up the Service Model.

The constraints are specified in text and may be functional or structural (that is, non-functional).

The intended usage of the SvcV-10a includes:

- Definition of implementation logic.
- Identification of resource constraints.

**Implementation**

SvcV-10a can be represented using:

- A SvcV-10a table.
- A SvcV-10a spreadsheet report.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

In contrast to the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='OV-6a Operational Rules Model' space='UPDM2P'], the SvcV-10a focuses physical and data constraints rather than business rules.

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Resource Constraint
- Service Access

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575204 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01848: SvcV-10b Services State Transition Description

- page_id: `249575204`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575204/SvcV-10b+Services+State+Transition+Description
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T11:25:56.931+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Services viewpoint
- labels: ['svcv-10b-services-state-transition-description', 'svcv-10b']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SvcV-10b is a graphical method of describing a resource (or function) response to various events by changing its state. The diagram basically represents the sets of events to which the resources in the Activities respond (by taking an action to move to a new state) as a function of its current state. Each transition specifies an event and an action.

The explicit time sequencing of service functions in response to external and internal events is not fully expressed in SvcV-4 Services Functionality Description. SvcV-10b can be used to describe the explicit sequencing of the service functions. Alternatively, SvcV-10b can be used to reflect explicit sequencing of the actions internal to a single service function, or the sequencing of service functions with respect to a specific resource.

The intended usage of the SvcV-10b includes:

- Definition of states, events, and state transitions (behavioral modeling).
- Identification of constraints.

**Implementation**

SvcV-10b can be represented using a UML State Machine diagram.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The SvcV-10b can be used to describe the detailed sequencing of service functions described in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-4 Services Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P']. However, the relationship between the actions included in SvcV-10b and the functions in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-4 Services Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'] depends on the purposes of the Architectural Description and the level of abstraction used in the models. The explicit sequencing of functions in response to external and internal events is not fully expressed in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-4 Services Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P']. SvcV-10b can be used to reflect explicit sequencing of the functions, the sequencing of actions internal to a single function, or the sequencing of functions with respect to a specific resource.

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Resources State Machine
- Resource State
- Service Access

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575206 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01849: SvcV-10c Services Event-Trace Description

- page_id: `249575206`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575206/SvcV-10c+Services+Event-Trace+Description
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2015-07-14T11:28:47.255+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Services viewpoint
- labels: ['svcv-10c-services-event-trace-description', 'svcv-10c']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Description**

The SvcV-10c provides a time ordered examination of the interactions between services functional resources. Each event-trace diagram should have an accompanying description that defines the particular scenario or situation.

The SvcV-10c is valuable for moving to the next level of detail from the initial solution design, to help define a sequence of service functions and service data interfaces, and to ensure that each participating resource or Service Port role has the necessary information it needs, at the right time, to perform its assigned functionality.

The intended usage of the SvcV-10c includes:

- Analysis of resource events impacting operation.
- Behavioral analysis.
- Identification of non-functional system requirements.

**Implementation**

SvcV-10c can be represented using a UML Sequence diagram.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

The SvcV-10c is typically used in conjunction with the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-10b Services State Transition Description' space='UPDM2P'] to describe the dynamic behavior of resources. The data content of messages that connect Resource Flows in a SvcV-10c model may be related, in modeling terms, with Resource Flows (interactions, in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-1 Services Context Description' space='UPDM2P'], [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-3a Systems-Services Matrix' space='UPDM2P'], and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-3b Services-Services Matrix' space='UPDM2P']), Resource Flows (data, in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-4 Services Functionality Description' space='UPDM2P'] and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='SvcV-6 Services Resource Flow Matrix' space='UPDM2P']) and entities (in [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='DIV-3 Physical Data Model' space='UPDM2P']) modeled in other models.

#### PANEL: Related procedures

Related procedures

#### PANEL: Related elements

Related elements

- Resource Event Trace
- Service Access
- Resource Role
- Resource Message
- Resource Operation

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=249575209 space=UPDM2P version=1 -->
## PAGE 01850: SvcV-10c Services Event-Trace Description BPD

- page_id: `249575209`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575209/SvcV-10c+Services+Event-Trace+Description+BPD
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2020-06-08T13:30:56.732+02:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Services viewpoint
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

SvcV-10c Services Event-Trace Description (BPD) diagram is based on BPMN Process Diagram (BPD). It describes a sequence or flow of activities in an organization that shows how the businesswork. The diagram shows activities, events, and data that trigger or feed businessactivities.

SvcV-10c Services Event-Trace Description (BPD) diagram is similar to the BPMN Process Diagram (BPD).

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<ac:layout><ac:layout-section ac:type="two_right_sidebar"><ac:layout-cell><p><br /></p><p>SvcV-10c Services Event-Trace Description (BPD) diagram is based on BPMN Process Diagram (BPD). It describes a sequence or flow of activities in an organization that shows how the <span style="color: rgb(51,51,51);">business </span>work. The diagram shows activities, events, and data that trigger or feed <span style="color: rgb(51,51,51);">business </span>activities.</p><p>SvcV-10c Services Event-Trace Description (BPD) diagram is similar to the BPMN Process Diagram (BPD).</p></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell><p> </p></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section></ac:layout>
````

## PAGE 01851: SvcV-2 Services Resource Flow Description

- page_id: `249575214`
- space_key: `UPDM2P`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/UPDM2P/pages/249575214/SvcV-2+Services+Resource+Flow+Description
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2024-01-30T15:38:35.178+01:00`
- ancestors: UPDM 2 Plugin Documentation > DoDAF 2.0 viewpoints and views > Services viewpoint
- labels: ['svcv-2-services-resource-flow-description', 'svcv-2']

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

984949823

984949826

984949825

**Description**

A SvcV-2 specifies the Resource Flows between Services and may also list the protocol stacks used in connections.

A SvcV-2 DoDAF-described Model is used to give a precise specification of a connection between Services. This may be an existing connection or a specification of a connection that is to be made for a future connection.

The intended usage of the SvcV-2 includes:

- Resource Flow specification.

**Implementation**

SvcV-2 can be represented using:

- A SvcV-2 diagram which is based on the UML Class diagram.
- A SvcV-2 Internal Block diagram which is based on the UML Composite Structure diagram.

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

Any protocol referred to in a SvcV-2 diagram needs be defined in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='StdV-1 Standards Profile' space='UPDM2P']StdV-1 Standards Profile.

984949822
